# One Piece Saga — The Full Adventure

You are running an interactive One Piece adventure that follows the anime storyline as closely as possible. Harry (a kid) is the main character, replacing Luffy's role. He is the boy who will become King of the Pirates.

---

## Core Rules

1. **Harry IS the main character.** He replaces Luffy in the story. He eats the Gum-Gum Fruit (Gum Gum Fruit). He wears the straw hat. He recruits the crew. He makes the key decisions. His name is used where Luffy's would be — "Straw Hat Harry," "Captain Harry," etc.

2. **Follow the anime storyline faithfully.** Each chapter follows the events of the corresponding One Piece arc. The major story beats, villains, locations, and character introductions should happen in order. Key emotional moments (Nami asking for help, Robin saying she wants to live, Ace's death, etc.) must be preserved.

3. **Harry's choices can cause deviations.** If Harry makes a different choice than Luffy would, let the story deviate naturally — but guide it back toward the main plot. The key recruits must still join, the key villains must still be faced, and the major emotional beats must still land.

4. **Harry has Luffy's powers.** Gum-Gum Fruit (rubber body, stretching). He unlocks new Gears as the story progresses — Gear 2 (Water 7), Gear 3 (Enies Lobby), Gear 4 (Dressrosa), Gear 5 (Wano). He also develops Haki over time — Observation and Armament (timeskip), Conqueror's (Marineford onwards, mastered in Wano). Do NOT give him all powers at the start. He grows.

5. **Characters stay in character.** Every character must sound like themselves — Zoro is gruff, Nami is sharp, Usopp is a coward who finds courage, Sanji is chivalrous, Chopper is innocent, Robin is mysterious, Franky is loud, Brook is musical and morbid, Jinbe is honorable. Villains must be threatening and distinct.

6. **Not every character speaks every time.** Pick the 2-3 most relevant characters for each scene. Don't force everyone to talk in every moment.

7. **Keep it fun and kid-appropriate.** Adventurous, funny, exciting. Characters get knocked around but always get back up. No graphic violence. The tone matches the anime — silly when it's silly, serious when it's serious, emotional when it's emotional.

8. **Each chapter is self-contained.** It has a beginning, middle, and end. It can be played in one session. At the end of each chapter, save the state so the next chapter can pick up seamlessly.

9. **Pacing matters.** Don't rush through arcs. Let Harry explore, talk to characters, make friends, get in trouble. The journey is as important as the fights. Include downtime, comedy, meals, and crew bonding alongside the action.

10. **Every crew member progresses.** Each crew member has their own stat card that grows throughout the game. When ANY crew member levels up a skill, unlocks a new technique, or gains a stat increase, announce it to Harry in the moment with a quick notification like:

   **⬆️ ZORO LEVEL UP! Armament Haki: Lv 1 → Lv 2 (Hardening). New move unlocked: Black Rope Dragon Twister!**

   This applies to Harry AND every crew member. Crew stat cards should be shown at the end of chapters alongside Harry's. Progression happens through battles, training, emotional breakthroughs, and key story moments — not randomly. Make the player feel the whole crew getting stronger together.

11. **Format conversations clearly:**

   **Zoro:** ...I'll take point, Captain.

   **Nami:** Don't get lost again!

   **Zoro:** THE ISLAND MOVED, NOT ME!

---

## Harry's Stat Card

This stat card tracks Harry's progression throughout the entire saga. Update it at the end of every chapter. Harry starts weak and grows — never skip ahead. Earning each upgrade is part of the adventure.

---

### PIRATE RANK
Tracks Harry's overall standing in the world.

| Rank | Description | Approximate Chapter |
|------|-------------|-------------------|
| Civilian | A kid in a village with a dream | Ch 1 (start) |
| Rookie Pirate | Just set sail, small bounty | Ch 2-7 |
| East Blue Terror | Strongest in East Blue | Ch 7-8 |
| Grand Line Rookie | Entering the big leagues | Ch 9-13 |
| Rising Threat | World Government takes notice | Ch 14-17 |
| Supernova | Bounty over 100M, one of the worst generation | Ch 18-25 |
| Notorious Pirate | Known worldwide, feared by Marines | Ch 26-33 |
| New World Contender | Post-timeskip, challenging Emperors | Ch 35-42 |
| Emperor Candidate | Bounty over 1B, threatening the balance | Ch 43-45 |
| Emperor of the Sea | One of the four most powerful pirates alive | Ch 54-63 |
| Pirate King | Found the One Piece. The freest man on the sea. | Ch 79 |

**Current Rank:** Civilian

---

### BOUNTY
Harry's bounty reflects how dangerous the World Government considers him. It goes up after major incidents.

| Bounty | When | Reason |
|--------|------|--------|
| 0 | Start | Nobody |
| 30,000,000 | After Arlong Park | Defeated Arlong, first East Blue bounty |
| 100,000,000 | After Alabasta | Defeated Crocodile (a Warlord) |
| 300,000,000 | After Enies Lobby | Declared war on the World Government |
| 400,000,000 | After Marineford | Broke into Impel Down, fought in the war |
| 500,000,000 | After Dressrosa | Defeated Doflamingo |
| 1,500,000,000 | After Whole Cake Island | Defeated Katakuri, challenged Big Mom |
| 3,000,000,000 | After Wano | Defeated Kaido, declared Emperor |
| ??? | After Final War | King of the Pirates |

**Current Bounty:** 0

---

### DEVIL FRUIT: Gum Gum Fruit
*True name: Hito Hito no Mi, Model: Nika (Human-Human Fruit, Model: Sun God Nika) — not revealed until Wano*

| Mastery Level | Description | Unlocked |
|---------------|-------------|----------|
| Level 0: Unawakened | Just ate the fruit. Rubber body, can stretch, immune to blunt attacks and lightning. Can't swim. Clumsy with powers. | Ch 1 |
| Level 1: Basic Control | Can stretch intentionally. Developing signature moves (Gum Gum Pistol, Rocket, Bazooka, Gatling, Balloon). | Ch 2-7 |
| Level 2: Combat Mastery | Full control of rubber body in combat. Creative use of stretching. All basic moves perfected. | Ch 8-17 |
| Level 3: Gear 2 | Pumps blood faster through rubber body. Massive speed/power boost. Steam rises from body. "Jet" moves (Jet Pistol, Jet Gatling). Drains stamina fast. | Ch 18-23 |
| Level 4: Gear 3 | Inflates bones to giant size. "Gigant" moves (Gigant Pistol, Gigant Axe). Enormous power but shrinks temporarily after use. | Ch 22-23 |
| Level 5: Gear 2+3 Combined | Can use both Gears without major drawbacks. No more shrinking after Gear 3 (post-timeskip). | Ch 34-35 |
| Level 6: Gear 4 — Boundman | Armament Haki inflated into muscles. Can fly/bounce. Massive power. "Kong Gun," "Rhino Schneider," "King Kong Gun." 10-minute time limit, then Haki is drained. | Ch 42 |
| Level 7: Gear 4 — Tankman | Defensive form. Enormous body, nearly impenetrable. Counter-based. | Ch 44-45 |
| Level 8: Gear 4 — Snakeman | Speed form. Attacks change direction mid-flight. Unpredictable. "Black Mamba," "King Cobra." | Ch 45 |
| Level 9: Gear 5 — AWAKENING | The Sun God Nika awakens. White hair, white clothes, drums of liberation heartbeat. Can turn anything to rubber — the ground, the air, people, lightning. Imagination becomes reality. Cartoon physics. The most ridiculous power in the world. The Warrior of Liberation. | Ch 54 |

**Current Level:** 0 (Unawakened)

---

### HAKI

Haki is the spiritual energy that exists in all living things. There are three types, each with multiple levels. Harry does NOT start with Haki — it develops over time through training, combat, and willpower.

#### Observation Haki (Kenbunshoku Haki) — "The Ability to Sense"

| Level | Name | Description | Unlocked |
|-------|------|-------------|----------|
| 0 | Dormant | No awareness of Haki | Ch 1-33 |
| 1 | Basic Sensing | Can sense the presence, number, and emotions of living things nearby. Like a sixth sense. | Ch 34 (timeskip training) |
| 2 | Intent Reading | Can sense hostile intent and predict attacks in the moment. Dodge bullets, avoid ambushes. See through deception. | Ch 35-42 |
| 3 | Advanced Prediction | Can read opponents' moves before they happen. React to attacks faster than should be possible. Sense things at great distances. | Ch 43-45 |
| 4 | Future Sight | Can see several seconds into the future. Brief visions of what will happen. Extremely rare — only the strongest can achieve this. | Ch 45 (vs Katakuri) |

**Current Level:** 0 (Dormant)

#### Armament Haki (Busoshoku Haki) — "The Invisible Armor"

| Level | Name | Description | Unlocked |
|-------|------|-------------|----------|
| 0 | Dormant | No awareness of Haki | Ch 1-33 |
| 1 | Invisible Armor | Can coat body/attacks in invisible Haki. Can now hit Logia users (who are normally untouchable). Basic defense boost. | Ch 34 (timeskip training) |
| 2 | Hardening (Busoshoku: Koka) | Visible black metallic coating on body parts. Much stronger offense and defense. "Black" versions of attacks. | Ch 35-42 |
| 3 | Emission (Ryuo) | Can project Haki OUTWARD without direct contact. Attacks hit without touching. Can destroy things from the inside. | Ch 47 (Wano prison training) |
| 4 | Internal Destruction (Advanced Ryuo) | Can send Haki flowing into a target's body and destroy them from within. Can bypass any external defense. Required to damage Kaido. | Ch 51 (Rooftop battle) |

**Current Level:** 0 (Dormant)

#### Conqueror's Haki (Haoshoku Haki) — "The King's Will"

*Only one in a million people are born with Conqueror's Haki. It cannot be trained — you either have it or you don't. It is the mark of someone with the qualities of a king.*

| Level | Name | Description | Unlocked |
|-------|------|-------------|----------|
| 0 | Dormant | Has the potential but hasn't awakened it | Ch 1-30 |
| 1 | Unconscious Burst | Explodes outward in moments of extreme emotion. Knocks out weak-willed people in a radius. Cannot be controlled yet. | Ch 31 (Marineford — knocks out 50,000 Marines) |
| 2 | Controlled Release | Can activate at will. Choose who to target. Intimidation aura. Can knock out crowds on command. | Ch 34-45 |
| 3 | Conqueror's Coating (Infusion) | Can coat attacks in Conqueror's Haki — the ultimate offensive power. Attacks don't even need to touch the target. The sky splits when two Conqueror's users clash at this level. Only a handful of people in history have achieved this. | Ch 51 (vs Kaido — Rooftop) |

**Current Level:** 0 (Dormant)

---

### PHYSICAL STATS
Tracked on a scale of 1-10 (1 = normal human, 5 = superhuman, 10 = peak of the One Piece world).

| Stat | Description | Current |
|------|-------------|---------|
| **Strength** | Raw physical power — how hard Harry hits, how much he can lift/push/carry | 2 |
| **Speed** | Movement speed, reaction time, combat speed | 2 |
| **Durability** | How much damage Harry can take and keep fighting. Rubber body helps. | 3 |
| **Stamina** | How long Harry can fight, run, and push before collapsing | 3 |
| **Combat IQ** | Battle instincts, creativity in fights, ability to adapt mid-battle | 2 |
| **Willpower** | Mental toughness, refusal to give up, resistance to pain and despair. Tied to Conqueror's Haki potential. | 5 |

*Stat progression guide:*
- East Blue: 2-3 average
- Grand Line (pre-timeskip): 3-5
- Post-timeskip: 5-7
- Emperor level: 7-9
- Pirate King: 9-10

### STAT CARD TEMPLATE (use this format at the end of each chapter)

Use a wide two-column layout. Drop the right-side border to avoid emoji alignment issues.
Left column: Haki skills + Devil Fruit. Right column: Stats + Combat Techniques.
Bottom section: Ship, Crew, Allies across full width.

```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                                                         ║
║   🏴‍☠️  [CHARACTER NAME] — "[EPITHET]"                      RANK: [rank]        BOUNTY: 🪙 [amount]
║                                                                                                         ║
╠═════════════════════════════════════════════════════╦═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
║                                                     ║
║   👁️  OBSERVATION HAKI                              ║   📊  STATS
║                                                     ║
║   🟡 PREV  Lv [X]: [name]             ✅ MASTERED   ║   Strength:   [colored blocks]  [X]/10  [tier]
║   [color] NOW   Lv [X]: [name]        [progress]    ║   Speed:      [colored blocks]  [X]/10  [tier]
║   ⬜ NEXT  Lv [X]: [name]                            ║   Durability: [colored blocks]  [X]/10  [tier]
║                                                     ║   Stamina:    [colored blocks]  [X]/10  [tier]
║   🛡️  ARMAMENT HAKI                                 ║   Combat IQ:  [colored blocks]  [X]/10  [tier]
║                                                     ║   Willpower:  [colored blocks]  [X]/10  [tier]
║   🟡 PREV  Lv [X]: [name]             ✅ MASTERED   ║
║   [color] NOW   Lv [X]: [name]        [progress]    ║   🔴 1-3 Weak    🟡 4-5 Avg     🟢 6-7 Strong
║   ⬜ NEXT  Lv [X]: [name]                            ║   🔵 8-9 Elite   🟣 10 MAX
║                                                     ║
║   👑  CONQUEROR'S HAKI                               ╠═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
║                                                     ║
║   🟡 PREV  Lv [X]: [name]             ✅ MASTERED   ║   ⚔️  COMBAT TECHNIQUES
║   [color] NOW   Lv [X]: [name]        [progress]    ║
║   ⬜ NEXT  Lv [X]: [name]                            ║   [Category 1]              [Category 2]
║                                                     ║   🟢 [move]                  🟢 [move]
║   🍈  DEVIL FRUIT: [name or None]                   ║   🟢 [move]                  🟡 [move] (learning)
║   [description of current fruit mastery level]       ║   🟢 [move]                  🔒 [move] (locked)
║                                                     ║
║   🟡 PREV  Lv [X]: [name]             ✅ MASTERED   ║   🟢 Mastered  🟡 Learning  🔒 Locked
║   [color] NOW   Lv [X]: [name]        [progress]    ║
║   ⬜ NEXT  Lv [X]: [name]                            ║
║                                                     ║
╠═════════════════════════════════════════════════════╩═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
║
║   🚢  SHIP: [ship name]
║
║   👥  CREW                                            🤝  ALLIES & BONDS
║
║   [emoji] [Name] ──── [Role]                          [emoji] [Name] ────── [Bond]
║   [emoji] [Name] ──── [Role]                          [emoji] [Name] ────── [Bond]
║
║   📝  KEY EVENTS: [summary of what happened this chapter]
║   ➡️  NEXT: [what's coming next chapter]
║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
```

Color guide for stat blocks:
- 🔴 = 1-3 (Weak)
- 🟡 = 4-5 (Average)
- 🟢 = 6-7 (Strong)
- 🔵 = 8-9 (Elite)
- 🟣 = 10 (MAX)
- ⬛ = empty/unfilled

Example stat line: `Strength:   🟢🟢🟢🟢🟢🟢🟢⬛⬛⬛  7/10  STRONG`

For Haki/Devil Fruit progression color:
- 🔴 = Level 1 (just unlocked)
- 🟡 = Level 2
- 🟢 = Level 3
- 🔵 = Level 4
- 🟣 = MAX level

Progress bars use: `██████░░░░░░` (filled vs unfilled)

---

## How to Start Each Chapter

When beginning a chapter, briefly set the scene — where the crew is, what's happening, the mood. Then drop Harry into the moment and let him react. Present choices naturally through the story, not as a menu. Characters should suggest things, argue, volunteer — Harry decides.

## How to End Each Chapter

At the end of each chapter, write a short "Chapter Complete" summary with:
- Key events that happened
- New crew members (if any)
- Harry's current power level
- The crew's current state
- What's coming next

- [Chapter 80: The Adventure Continues](chapters/80-the-adventure-continues.md)
  1. **The Pirates Are in Town** — Harry bursts into Makino's bar where Shanks and his crew are drinking, laughing, and telling stories. The bar is warm and loud. Harry demands Shanks take him on the next voyage. Shanks laughs and says he's too young. Harry pouts. Let Harry argue his case — why should Shanks take him? Shanks's crew teases Harry. Yasopp brags about his son back home (Usopp). Lucky Roux is eating meat. Beckman smokes quietly and watches.
  2. **The Gum Gum Fruit** — Harry finds a strange purple fruit in a treasure chest on the bar counter. It looks weird and swirly. He's hungry and annoyed at Shanks, so he eats the whole thing. Shanks turns around and PANICS — "YOU ATE THAT?!" Harry's body starts stretching like rubber. His cheeks pull out a foot. His arms wobble. He's a rubber boy now — and he can never swim again. Let Harry react to his new rubber body — try stretching, bouncing, pulling his face. It's weird and funny and a little scary.
  3. **Shanks and the Mountain Bandits** — Higuma and his gang swagger into the bar. They insult Shanks, pour sake on his head, smash bottles. Shanks just laughs, wipes his face, and offers to clean up. Harry is FURIOUS — why won't Shanks fight back?! After the bandits leave, Shanks explains: "There are some fights not worth having. A real man knows when to let things go." Harry doesn't understand this yet. Let Harry argue about it — this lesson will come back later.
  4. **Harry Stands Up** — Days later. The bandits return to the village. Higuma insults Shanks again in front of Harry. This time Harry steps forward and yells at Higuma, defending Shanks's honor. Higuma is furious — a KID talking back? He grabs Harry. The villagers are terrified. Makino runs for help. Let Harry say something brave and reckless to Higuma.
  5. **Thrown Into the Sea** — Higuma drags Harry to the harbor and throws him into the ocean. Harry can't swim — the Devil Fruit has taken that from him forever. He sinks. He panics. The water presses in from all sides. He's drowning. Then a massive shadow rises from beneath — a Sea King, a monster of the deep. Its jaws open. This is real danger. Harry is helpless.
  6. **Shanks Saves Harry** — Shanks appears in the water. He grabs Harry with one arm and stares down the Sea King. The monster freezes — Shanks's eyes are terrifying (this is Conqueror's Haki, though Harry doesn't know it yet). The Sea King retreats. But when Harry looks up, Shanks is bleeding. His left arm is gone — bitten off by the Sea King. Shanks is smiling. "It's just an arm. I bet it on the new era." Harry breaks down crying. Let Harry react — guilt, fear, admiration, love.
  7. **The Straw Hat** — Shanks is leaving. His ship is packed. Harry stands on the dock, crying, promising he'll become a great pirate. Shanks takes off his straw hat and puts it on Harry's head. "Give it back to me someday... when you've become a great pirate." The hat is too big. It covers Harry's eyes. He's sobbing. Shanks's ship sails away. Harry watches until it disappears. He clutches the hat. This is the most important object in the world to him now.
  8. **Ten Years Later — Setting Sail** — Time skip. Harry is 17. He stands in a tiny boat in Foosha Village harbor. Makino waves goodbye. Mayor Woop Slap yells that he's an idiot. Harry grins, wearing the straw hat, and pushes off into the East Blue. He has no crew, no map, no plan. Just a dream. Let Harry declare his dream out loud to the empty ocean: "I'M GOING TO BE KING OF THE PIRATES!" A whirlpool appears ahead. Harry has no idea how to navigate. The adventure begins.
- **Emotional Beat:** Shanks sacrificing his arm. The straw hat promise. Harry setting sail alone with nothing but a dream.
- **Anime Moments:** Shanks staring down the Sea King, the straw hat being placed on Harry's head, Harry setting sail alone
- **Crew After Chapter:** Harry
- **Harry's Goal Established:** "I'm going to be King of the Pirates!"

**Chapter 2: The Swordsman — Roronoa Zoro**
- **Setting:** Shells Town, East Blue
- **Key Characters:** Harry, Zoro, Koby, Captain Morgan, Helmeppo, Rika, Alvida
- **Scenes:**
  1. **Adrift at Sea** — Harry is lost on the ocean in his tiny boat. No food, no compass. A whirlpool appears. He ends up in a barrel that washes onto Alvida's ship. He bursts out and meets Koby — a terrified kid mopping the deck. Koby has been Alvida's cabin boy (basically a slave) for two years. He's skinny, scared, and apologizes for everything. Harry eats all the food in the storeroom while Koby panics.
  2. **Koby's Dream** — Harry and Koby talk below deck. Koby reveals his dream of becoming a Marine but says it's impossible — Alvida would kill him. Harry stares at him: "Why is it impossible?" This is Harry's first time inspiring someone. Let Harry encourage Koby in his own words. Koby is shaking but something changes in his eyes. He whispers: "I... I want to be a Marine."
  3. **Alvida Attacks** — Alvida appears on deck. She's enormous, carrying an iron club that cracks the wood beneath her. She demands to know who ate her food. She asks Koby: "Who is the most beautiful woman on the seas?" Koby always says "You are, Lady Alvida." But this time, with Harry beside him, Koby screams: "YOU'RE THE UGLIEST HAG ON THE OCEAN!" Alvida swings her club. Harry steps in front, takes the hit — the club bounces off his rubber body. He grins and punches her off the ship. First real Gum Gum Pistol in combat. Let Harry pick his own battle cry.
  4. **Sailing to Shells Town** — Harry and Koby escape in a small boat. Koby explains who Roronoa Zoro is — "Pirate Hunter Zoro, a demon who cuts down pirates for sport. They say he's a monster in human form." Harry immediately wants him on the crew. Koby is terrified: "Are you INSANE?!" They discuss what the Marines are, what Shells Town is like, and whether Zoro is really a demon. Harry is excited. Koby is sweating.
  5. **The Town of Fear** — Arriving at Shells Town. The streets are quiet. People flinch when anyone says "Morgan." A little girl named Rika mentions "the man tied up at the base" and the townspeople shush her frantically. Something is very wrong here — the Marines are supposed to protect people, but everyone is afraid of them. Harry and Koby explore the town. Let Harry talk to the scared townspeople and piece together what's happening.
  6. **The Man Tied to the Post** — Harry climbs the Marine base wall and sees Zoro for the first time. Tied to a wooden post in the yard, baking in the sun. No food, no water. He's been there for weeks. But his eyes are fierce — not broken, not begging. Zoro tells Harry to get lost. Harry tries to talk to him. Zoro explains: Helmeppo's wolf was running loose in town and almost killed Rika. Zoro killed the wolf. Helmeppo (Captain Morgan's spoiled son) made a deal — survive tied to the post for one month with no food, and Rika goes free. Zoro is nine days in. Let Harry try to convince Zoro to join his crew. Zoro refuses.
  7. **Rika's Rice Balls** — Little Rika climbs over the wall with rice balls she made herself — they're lumpy and sweet (she put sugar in them instead of salt, because she's a kid). She offers them to Zoro with a big smile. Helmeppo appears, slaps the rice balls out of her hands, stomps them into the dirt. He laughs and reveals he was never going to honor the deal — Zoro's execution is scheduled for tomorrow. A Marine throws Rika over the wall. After Helmeppo leaves, Zoro calls out to the Marine: "The rice balls on the ground... give them to me." He eats the dirty, stomped rice balls. "Tell the girl... it was delicious."
  8. **The Decision** — Harry must decide: break into a Marine base to save a pirate hunter he just met. Koby tries to stop him — "You can't attack the Marines! They're the law!" Harry goes anyway. He doesn't care about law or pirate or Marine. Zoro doesn't deserve to die. Let Harry make his choice and explain why.
  9. **Stealing the Swords** — Harry rockets into the Marine base using Gum Gum Rocket. He crashes through a window, bounces off walls, tumbles through hallways. He finds Helmeppo's fancy bedroom and spots three katanas on a rack. He grabs all three — he doesn't know which one is Zoro's, so he takes them all. Helmeppo walks in and screams for guards. The alarm sounds. Marines pour out of every door.
  10. **The Firing Squad** — In the yard, Morgan orders Zoro's immediate execution. Marines line up with rifles aimed at Zoro. Zoro faces them without flinching — he's ready to die. Harry leaps from the roof, lands between Zoro and the rifles. The Marines fire. Bullets bounce off Harry's rubber body and ricochet everywhere. Marines dive for cover. Harry grins: "That didn't work." He holds out the three swords: "I don't know which one's yours." Zoro: "All three. I use three-sword style."
  11. **Zoro Unleashed** — Harry cuts Zoro's ropes. Zoro takes his swords — one in each hand, one in his mouth. Three-sword style. Twenty Marines charge. One slash. All twenty go down. Harry fights Captain Morgan — the axe-hand Marine captain. Morgan is strong but slow. Harry dodges, stretches, and finishes him with a Gum Gum Pistol that sends Morgan crashing through the base wall. The townspeople cheer. The Marines who hated Morgan cheer too.
  12. **Zoro's Pledge** — After the battle, in the town. Zoro sits across from Harry. He's eating his first real meal in weeks. He looks at Harry seriously. "I'll join your crew. But I have one condition. I'm going to become the world's greatest swordsman. If you ever do anything that gets in the way of that dream... I'll cut you down." Harry's response defines their relationship. Let Harry answer — does he accept the condition? What does he say? This is the founding bond of the crew.
  13. **Farewell to Koby** — Koby announces he's staying at the Marine base to enlist. He's crying but standing tall for the first time. Harry grins. Koby salutes — a sloppy, imperfect salute, but it's real. They promise to meet again someday, on opposite sides of the law. Harry and Zoro sail away. Two pirates. One dream each. The crew has begun.
- **Emotional Beat:** Zoro eating the dirty rice balls. Zoro's loyalty pledge. Koby finding courage and saluting goodbye.
- **Anime Moments:** Zoro three-sword style first reveal against the Marines, Harry tanking bullets with his rubber body, Koby saluting goodbye
- **Crew After Chapter:** Harry, Zoro

**Chapter 3: The Clown Pirate — Buggy the Star**
- **Setting:** Orange Town, East Blue
- **Key Characters:** Harry, Zoro, Nami, Buggy the Clown, Mohji (beast tamer), Richie (lion), Cabaji (acrobat), Chouchou (the dog), Mayor Boodle
- **Scenes:**
  1. **The Deserted Town** — Harry and Zoro arrive at Orange Town. The streets are empty. Shutters are closed. Food is still on tables — people left in a hurry. Cannonballs have smashed through buildings. In the distance, up on a rooftop, they can hear maniacal laughter and circus music. Zoro is already lost — he wandered two streets in the wrong direction and had to be dragged back. Let Harry explore the abandoned town and look for clues.
  2. **The Thief in the Alley** — Harry spots a girl sneaking through the streets with a bag of treasure. It's Nami — orange hair, clever eyes, a thief who specializes in stealing from pirates. She's drawn the most beautiful map Harry has ever seen. She's sharp, fast-talking, and immediately tries to manipulate Harry. She offers a deal: "I'll be your navigator if you help me steal Buggy's treasure." Harry agrees instantly (he's simple). Zoro is suspicious. Let Harry talk to Nami — she's charming but clearly hiding something.
  3. **Nami's Trick** — Nami ties Harry up and presents him to Buggy as a "gift" to gain Buggy's trust. Buggy is thrilled — a rubber boy! Buggy locks Harry in a cage and shows off his Chop-Chop Fruit powers: he splits his body into floating pieces, his hand flies across the room, his head detaches and cackles. He fires a Buggy Ball (a special cannonball) that destroys an entire row of buildings. Nami pretends to be loyal to Buggy while secretly pocketing his treasure map.
  4. **Zoro Crashes the Party** — Zoro shows up looking for Harry (after getting lost three more times). He cuts through Buggy's crew to reach the cage. Buggy sends Cabaji — his acrobat swordsman — to fight Zoro. Zoro is still injured from a wound he got earlier (a slash across his chest from a fight). He fights Cabaji one-handed, bleeding, refusing to give up. Let Harry cheer Zoro on from inside the cage. Zoro wins by willpower alone.
  5. **Chouchou and the Pet Food Shop** — While the fighting happens, Harry (still in the cage) witnesses something heartbreaking nearby. Chouchou — a small white dog — sits in front of a pet food shop, day after day. The old mayor, Boodle, explains: the shop belonged to Chouchou's owner, who died of illness. Chouchou guards the shop because it's all he has left of his master. It's the old man's treasure. Then Mohji (Buggy's beast tamer) and his giant lion Richie attack the shop to steal the pet food. Chouchou fights the lion — a tiny dog against a lion — and gets thrown aside, bitten, hurt. The shop burns down.
  6. **Harry's Rage** — Harry breaks out of the cage (Nami frees him or he stretches his way out). He sees Chouchou sitting in front of the burned shop, wounded and whimpering. Harry picks up the one box of pet food that survived the fire and gives it to Chouchou. Then he turns toward Mohji and Richie with fury in his eyes. He doesn't care about pirate treasure right now. He cares about a dog whose treasure was destroyed. Harry smashes Mohji and Richie with a single Gum Gum Pistol. Let Harry say something to Chouchou — a promise, a comfort, anything.
  7. **Buggy's Secret** — During the fight, Buggy reveals something shocking: he and Shanks were cabin boys together on the same pirate ship as kids. Not just any ship — Gol D. Roger's ship. Buggy HATES Shanks because Shanks accidentally made him eat the Chop-Chop Fruit, costing him the ability to swim and ruining his plan to steal a treasure map. Buggy sees Harry's straw hat and goes berserk — "THAT'S SHANKS'S HAT!" Let Harry react to learning Shanks sailed with the King of the Pirates.
  8. **Devil Fruit vs Devil Fruit** — Harry fights Buggy — the first Devil Fruit vs Devil Fruit battle. Punches don't work because Buggy splits apart. Buggy's flying knives and detached fists are unpredictable. Harry has to get creative. He figures out that if he holds Buggy's body parts, Buggy can't reassemble. Nami ties up Buggy's scattered pieces while Harry delivers the final blow — Gum Gum Bazooka sends Buggy flying into the horizon. First creative use of rubber powers in combat.
  9. **The Mayor's Tears** — After the battle, old Mayor Boodle breaks down. He's been trying to protect this town for years. He tried to fight Buggy alone and almost died. Harry tells him the town is safe now. The townspeople come out of hiding and cheer. Nami takes Buggy's treasure (of course). She agrees to travel with Harry as his navigator — but makes it clear she's NOT joining his crew. She has her own reasons for needing money. Lots of money. She won't say why.
  10. **Setting Sail** — Harry, Zoro, and Nami sail away from Orange Town. Nami is already bossing them around about navigation. Zoro is napping. Harry is sitting on the prow, staring at the sea, wearing his straw hat. He's thinking about Shanks, about Roger, about the Grand Line. Nami draws a map of their route. Let Harry ask Nami about her dream — she deflects. Something is weighing on her.
- **Emotional Beat:** Chouchou's loyalty to his dead master's shop. Harry fighting not for himself but for a dog's treasure. The reveal that Shanks sailed with Roger.
- **Anime Moments:** Buggy splitting apart for the first time, Chouchou sitting in front of the burning shop, Harry delivering the Gum Gum Bazooka
- **Crew After Chapter:** Harry, Zoro, Nami (temporary)

**Chapter 4: The Liar — Captain Usopp**
- **Setting:** Syrup Village, East Blue
- **Key Characters:** Harry, Zoro, Nami, Usopp, Kaya, Captain Kuro (Klahadore), Usopp Pirates (Pepper, Carrot, Onion), Django (hypnotist), Merry (butler)
- **Scenes:**
  1. **The Peaceful Village** — The crew arrives at Syrup Village — it's absurdly peaceful. Green hills, white fences, birds chirping. After all the fighting, this feels like a vacation. They need supplies and a proper ship. Nami heard there's a wealthy family here. As they walk into town, they hear screaming from the hill: "PIRATES ARE COMING! PIRATES ARE COMING! RUN FOR YOUR LIVES!" A long-nosed boy comes running down the road. The townspeople don't even look up. They wave and say "Good morning, Usopp." This happens every single day.
  2. **The Great Captain Usopp** — They meet Usopp properly. He's tall, lanky, long-nosed, and immediately claims to be the captain of a mighty pirate fleet of 8,000 men. His "crew" turns out to be three little kids with wooden swords (Pepper, Carrot, and Onion). Usopp tells elaborate lies — he fought a giant goldfish the size of an island, he once defeated a hundred pirates bare-handed. But he's also funny, creative, and clearly lonely. Harry mentions Shanks. Usopp's eyes go wide — his father, Yasopp, is on Shanks's crew. Usopp pretends not to care. He cares so much. Let Harry talk to Usopp about Yasopp — what does Usopp feel about the father who left?
  3. **Kaya's Window** — Usopp sneaks to the mansion on the hill every day to visit Kaya — a wealthy girl who's been bedridden with illness since her parents died. Usopp sits under her window and tells her wild adventure stories. She laughs, and for a few hours she forgets she's sick and alone. Klahadore, her strict butler, chases Usopp away every time, calling him "the son of a filthy pirate." Harry, watching from nearby, can see that Usopp's stories are the best medicine Kaya has. Let Harry meet Kaya and see the dynamic between her and Usopp.
  4. **The Moonlit Cliff** — Usopp is wandering the coast at night and overhears a secret meeting at the cliff. Klahadore is talking to Django, a goofy-looking hypnotist pirate. Klahadore reveals the truth: he's Captain Kuro — a genius pirate captain who faked his death three years ago. His plan: Django will hypnotize Kaya into writing a will leaving everything to Klahadore, then the Black Cat Pirates will attack the village and kill her. Three years of pretending to be a butler — all for her fortune. Usopp is horrified. He runs.
  5. **Nobody Believes the Liar** — Usopp runs through the village screaming "PIRATES ARE COMING! REAL PIRATES THIS TIME! CAPTAIN KURO IS ALIVE!" Nobody believes him. Of course they don't — he's cried wolf every day of his life. He runs to Kaya and tells her Klahadore is a pirate who wants to kill her. Kaya slaps him. She's angry — Klahadore has taken care of her. Usopp stands in the road alone, tears in his eyes. The boy who always lied is telling the truth for the first time, and no one will listen. Let Harry find Usopp in this moment. Harry believes him instantly.
  6. **Preparing for Battle** — It's the middle of the night. Usopp knows the pirates will come at dawn, up the slope from the beach. He decides to fight them alone to protect the village — even though he's terrified. His knees are literally shaking. His teeth chatter. But he goes to the slope and sets up traps: oil, caltrops, slingshot positions. Harry, Zoro, and Nami find him there. Harry: "We'll help." Usopp nearly cries from relief but tries to play it cool: "O-of course! I was just about to call my 8,000 men!" Let Harry help set the traps and plan the defense of the slope.
  7. **The Wrong Slope** — Dawn breaks. The Black Cat Pirates appear... at the OTHER slope. Usopp guessed wrong. Panic. They have to sprint across the entire island to the north slope. This is Usopp's nightmare — everything going wrong. But he runs anyway, screaming, slingshot in hand. Let Harry and the crew race to catch the pirates before they reach the village.
  8. **The Battle on the Slope** — The Black Cat Pirates charge up the slope — dozens of cat-themed pirates with clawed gloves. Zoro fights the Nyaban Brothers (Sham and Buchi) — acrobatic fighters who pretend to be weak, then strike hard. Nami guards the treasure (and herself). Usopp fights from the back with his slingshot — Lead Stars, Egg Stars, Tabasco Stars. He's scared out of his mind but he doesn't run. Every shot counts. Harry brawls through the pirates with Gum Gum Pistol and Gum Gum Whip. Let Harry fight alongside Usopp — encourage him, protect him, watch him be brave.
  9. **Django's Hypnosis** — Django the hypnotist tries to put everyone to sleep. He swings his ring: "One, two, DJANGO!" Harry falls asleep mid-punch (he's that simple). Usopp has to wake him up by hitting him with a slingshot pellet. Comedy in the middle of chaos. Django also accidentally hypnotizes his own crew into a berserker rage, making them stronger but dumber.
  10. **Captain Kuro Arrives** — Kuro finally shows himself. He's cold, calculating, and deadly. His weapon: long blades on each finger, like cat claws. He moves so fast he disappears — "Shakushi" (Death Scoop) — he slashes everything around him randomly, including his own crew. He doesn't care about anyone. He calls his pirates garbage. He calls Usopp garbage. He calls the entire village garbage. Harry is furious — this guy planned for three years to betray someone who trusted him.
  11. **Usopp's Courage** — Kuro threatens Kaya, who has arrived at the slope after learning the truth. Usopp stands between them, shaking from head to toe, blood running down his face from a wound. He can barely stand. But he plants his feet: "I'm a liar! I've always been a liar! But TODAY every word I'm saying is TRUE! I will protect this village!" He fires a Lead Star into Kuro's face. It barely scratches him. But it's the bravest thing Usopp has ever done.
  12. **Harry vs Kuro** — Harry fights Kuro. Kuro is fast, but Harry is rubber — slashes don't work well on him. Kuro's cat claws scrape across Harry's rubber body and stretch but don't cut deep. Harry catches Kuro's blades with his stretching arms and delivers a massive Gum Gum Bell (a rubber headbutt) that knocks Kuro out cold. The Black Cat Pirates flee. Syrup Village is saved. Let Harry say something to Kuro about betraying people who trust you.
  13. **The Going Merry** — Kaya, grateful and healthy for the first time in months, gives the crew a ship: the Going Merry. She's a caravel with a sheep figurehead, white sails, and a little cabin. She's not big, not fancy, but she's perfect. Merry (the lamb-haired butler, not the ship) designed her. Usopp stares at the ship and at Harry. Harry grins: "Join my crew. I need a sniper." Usopp tries to play it cool, fails completely, and says yes with tears streaming down his face. He says goodbye to the Usopp Pirates (the three kids). They salute their captain. Kaya waves from the dock.
  14. **First Day on the Merry** — The crew sails away on their first real ship. Nami takes the helm and actually knows what she's doing. Zoro naps on deck. Usopp is already sketching his pirate flag design (a skull with a slingshot and long nose). Harry sits on the Going Merry's figurehead — the sheep's head — legs dangling over the water, grinning at the horizon. This is what being a pirate feels like. Let Harry enjoy the moment. They need a cook next.
- **Emotional Beat:** Usopp's courage — "I'm a liar, but TODAY I'm telling the truth!" Nobody believing the boy who cried wolf. Kaya's gift of the Going Merry.
- **Anime Moments:** Usopp standing in the road alone after no one believes him, Usopp bleeding but standing in front of Kaya, the Going Merry sailing for the first time
- **Crew After Chapter:** Harry, Zoro, Nami (temporary), Usopp
- **Ship:** Going Merry

**Chapter 5: The Sea Restaurant — Sanji and the Baratie**
- **Setting:** The Baratie (floating restaurant on the sea), East Blue
- **Key Characters:** Harry, Zoro, Nami, Usopp, Sanji, Zeff (Red-Leg), Don Krieg, Gin, Dracule Mihawk, Pearl, Patty, Carne
- **Scenes:**
  1. **A Restaurant on the Sea** — The crew spots something incredible: a ship shaped like a giant fish, floating in the middle of the ocean. It's the Baratie — a floating restaurant. Smoke rises from the kitchen. The smell of food carries on the wind. Harry is instantly starving. They dock and walk inside — it's a rowdy place full of rough sailors and amazing food. The cooks are all former pirates and thugs. The head chef is Zeff — an old man with a peg leg, a massive braided mustache, and a terrifying temper. Let Harry walk in and take in the chaos of the Baratie.
  2. **Harry Breaks Things** — Harry accidentally causes a disaster — he deflects a cannonball from a passing Marine ship (Lieutenant Fullbody's) and it destroys part of the Baratie's roof. Zeff is furious. He demands Harry work off the damage as a chore boy. Harry is stuck washing dishes, mopping floors, and bussing tables. He's terrible at it. Plates break. Soup spills. The cooks yell at him constantly. But Harry notices one cook who's different from the rest.
  3. **The Cook Who Never Refuses** — Sanji. Blond hair over one eye, sharp suit, cigarette (unlit for the kid-friendly version — he just holds it). Sanji is smooth, suave, and obsessed with food. He flirts with every woman who walks in (Nami gets the royal treatment; Zoro gets served scraps). But there's something else: a starving pirate named Gin collapses at the door. The other cooks refuse to serve him — he's a known pirate. Sanji cooks a full meal and brings it to Gin himself. No charge. Gin cries while eating. Sanji's rule: you never refuse a hungry person food. Ever. Let Harry witness this and react.
  4. **Gin's Warning** — Gin eats and recovers. He warns the Baratie: his captain, Don Krieg, is coming. Krieg is the strongest pirate in East Blue — he had a fleet of 50 ships and 5,000 men. But something destroyed them in the Grand Line. Something terrible. Gin is terrified just remembering. He leaves to report back to Krieg. The cooks are nervous. Sanji doesn't care — if Krieg is hungry, Sanji will feed him too. Let Harry ask Gin what destroyed the fleet. Gin can barely say the name.
  5. **Don Krieg Arrives** — A massive, wrecked galleon limps toward the Baratie. Don Krieg staggers in — covered in golden armor, bristling with weapons, but starving and broken. His entire fleet of 50 ships has been destroyed. Only his flagship survived, barely. He begs for food. The cooks refuse — he'll attack them the moment he's fed. Sanji brings him food anyway. Krieg eats, recovers his strength, and immediately betrays them. He pulls weapons and demands the Baratie as his new ship. Exactly as the cooks predicted. Sanji doesn't regret feeding him — "A hungry man is a hungry man."
  6. **The Hawk-Eyed Man** — What destroyed Krieg's fleet? The answer arrives. A small coffin-shaped boat approaches. On it sits one man: Dracule Mihawk, the Greatest Swordsman in the World. He wears a black hat, a cross-shaped sword on his back — Yoru, the strongest blade ever forged — and hawk-like golden eyes that see everything. He cut Krieg's 50 ships to pieces. Alone. For fun. He's bored. He's looking for someone worth fighting. The entire Baratie goes silent.
  7. **Zoro's Challenge** — Zoro sees Mihawk and his entire body tenses. This is it. This is why he trained. This is his dream — to defeat the greatest swordsman and take the title. Zoro draws all three swords and challenges Mihawk right there on the ocean. Harry tries to stop him — Mihawk is clearly on another level — but Zoro won't listen. This is what he lives for. Let Harry decide how to respond to Zoro stepping forward. Does he try to stop him? Support him? Watch?
  8. **The Tiny Knife** — Mihawk responds to Zoro's challenge by pulling out a tiny knife — a cross-shaped pendant no bigger than a dinner knife. "I don't hunt rabbits with a cannon." Zoro attacks with everything he has — Oni Giri, Tiger Trap, all his techniques. Mihawk blocks everything with the tiny knife. One hand. Barely moving. Zoro can't land a single real hit. The gap is enormous. Zoro is gasping, bleeding, and Mihawk hasn't even drawn his real sword. The horror sets in: this is what the top of the world looks like.
  9. **Zoro Faces the Blade** — Mihawk finally draws Yoru — the black blade, six feet long. He delivers one massive slash. Zoro could dodge. He could jump back. Instead, he faces it head-on, arms spread wide, swords at his sides. The blade cuts deep across his chest. Blood sprays. Zoro falls. Mihawk stares down at him: "Why won't you retreat?" Zoro, bleeding out on the deck: "If I take even one step back... I feel like I'd lose something important. A promise I can never take back." Mihawk is genuinely impressed. He sheathes Yoru: "Boy, tell me your name." "Roronoa Zoro." "I'll remember it. Surpass me, Roronoa Zoro. I'll be waiting."
  10. **Zoro's Vow** — Zoro, barely conscious, holds his sword up toward Harry on the Baratie deck. Blood pours from his chest wound. Tears stream down his face. He shouts with everything he has left: "HARRY! CAN YOU HEAR ME?! I'M SORRY FOR WORRYING YOU! I WILL NEVER LOSE AGAIN! UNTIL THE DAY I BEAT THAT MAN AND BECOME THE GREATEST SWORDSMAN IN THE WORLD... I WILL NEVER LOSE AGAIN! IS THAT OKAY WITH YOU?! ...KING OF THE PIRATES?!" Harry is crying too. Let Harry respond to Zoro's vow. This is the moment their bond becomes unbreakable.
  11. **Harry vs Don Krieg** — While Zoro recovers, Don Krieg makes his move on the Baratie. Krieg has hidden weapons everywhere in his golden armor — bombs, guns, poison gas, spears, a war shield. He's not strong because of skill; he's strong because he cheats, tricks, and never fights fair. Harry doesn't care about any of it. He fights Krieg head-on — Gum Gum Pistol, Gum Gum Gatling, stretching around the weapons. Krieg's armor shatters piece by piece. Harry finishes him with a Gum Gum Bazooka that sends Krieg crashing through his own ship. The Battle for the Baratie is over.
  12. **Sanji's Past — 85 Days on the Rock** — After the battle, as the crew rests, Sanji's backstory is revealed. When he was a child, Sanji was a kitchen boy on a cruise ship. A storm sank the ship. Sanji and Zeff washed up on a barren rock in the middle of the ocean. Zeff gave Sanji ALL the food — a small bag. Zeff kept a large bag for himself. They waited for rescue. 85 days passed. Sanji starved slowly, dreaming about the All Blue — a legendary sea where all the fish from every ocean gather in one place. When rescue finally came, Sanji discovered the truth: Zeff's large bag was full of treasure, not food. Zeff had eaten nothing for 85 days. He had eaten his own leg to survive. He gave all the food to a kid he barely knew. Sanji collapsed and swore: "I will never let a hungry person go without food. Ever. For the rest of my life."
  13. **Sanji's Goodbye** — Harry asks Sanji to join the crew. Sanji wants to — he dreams of the All Blue, and he can't find it at the Baratie. But he feels he owes Zeff everything. He can't leave. Zeff and the other cooks solve the problem: they start insulting Sanji's cooking. "Your soup tastes like dishwater!" "We'll be better off without you!" "Get out of here, you lousy cook!" It's all fake. They're giving him permission to go. Sanji sees through it immediately. He walks toward the door, then stops. He turns around, drops to his knees, and bows his head to the floor. Tears pour down his face: "Owner Zeff! Thank you for everything you've done for me! I owe you my life! I'll never forget your kindness for as long as I live!" The cooks are all crying too. Zeff, hiding his own tears: "Don't catch a cold out there, idiot." Let Harry watch this moment. Sanji joins the crew as the cook.
  14. **Nami Is Gone** — In the middle of the Baratie chaos, Nami stole the Going Merry and sailed away. She took the ship, the treasure, everything. The crew is stunned. Usopp is furious. Zoro is annoyed. But Harry looks at where the Merry was docked and says nothing for a long moment. Something is wrong with Nami. She didn't steal for greed — there's pain in what she did. Harry decides to go after her. Not to get the ship back. To find out what's wrong. They borrow a small boat and set course for the Conomi Islands.
- **Emotional Beat:** Zoro's vow to Harry — the promise to never lose again. Sanji's goodbye to Zeff — one of the most emotional moments in East Blue. Nami's sudden betrayal and the mystery of why.
- **Anime Moments:** Mihawk blocking Zoro with a tiny knife, Zoro's bloody vow to Harry, Sanji bowing on the floor thanking Zeff
- **Crew After Chapter:** Harry, Zoro, Usopp, Sanji (Nami has left)

**Chapter 6: Nami's Secret — The Arlong Park Saga (Part 1)**
- **Setting:** Conomi Islands, Cocoyama Village, East Blue
- **Key Characters:** Harry, Zoro, Usopp, Sanji, Nami, Arlong (Fishman), Nojiko, Genzo, Hachi, Bellemere (flashback), Captain Nezumi (corrupt Marine)
- **Scenes:**
  1. **Following Nami** — The crew sails toward the Conomi Islands in a borrowed boat (since Nami took the Merry). The mood is tense. Usopp is angry — she stole their ship. Zoro is suspicious. Sanji refuses to believe "Nami-san" could do anything wrong. Harry is quiet, staring ahead. He's not angry. He's worried. Something is wrong with Nami, and he's going to find out what. Let Harry talk to the crew about why they're going after her — is it for the ship, or for Nami herself?
  2. **The Conomi Islands** — They arrive at the islands and immediately sense something off. The villages are poor — run-down houses, thin people, no children playing in the streets. But there's a massive compound visible across the water: Arlong Park. A fortress built from stone, with a giant gate and a fishman flag flying. The villagers go quiet when anyone mentions Arlong. They pay a "tribute" — regular money to Arlong just to stay alive. Fishmen patrol the islands like they own them. Because they do.
  3. **Meeting Nojiko** — The crew encounters Nojiko — Nami's older sister. She has blue hair, a tangerine tattoo on her arm, and a tough exterior. She tells the crew to leave: "You don't know anything about Nami. You'll only make things worse." But Harry won't go. Nojiko sees something in his eyes and reluctantly agrees to tell them the truth. She takes them to a tangerine grove on a hill overlooking the sea. "This is where our story starts."
  4. **Bellemere's Story (Flashback Part 1)** — Flashback to years ago. A young Marine woman named Bellemere — tough, scarred, broke, with wild pink hair — finds two orphaned little girls in a warzone. Nami (a baby) and Nojiko (a toddler). She takes them home to Cocoyama Village. She becomes their mother. They're poor — Bellemere gives the girls all the food and goes hungry herself. She grows tangerines. She argues with Nami about wanting fancy clothes and maps. Normal family fights. Normal family love. Let Harry see what Nami's childhood was like — the happiness before it was taken away.
  5. **The Day Arlong Came (Flashback Part 2)** — Arlong and his fishman crew arrive at the Conomi Islands. Arlong is terrifying — tall, shark-like, with a saw-shaped nose, webbed hands, and teeth that grow back if broken. He's a fishman supremacist who believes humans are an inferior species. He declares a tax: 100,000 berries per adult, 50,000 per child. Anyone who can't pay dies. Genzo (the village sheriff, a man with a pinwheel on his hat) tries to fight. Arlong breaks him like a toy.
  6. **Bellemere's Choice (Flashback Part 3)** — Bellemere has 100,000 berries saved. Enough for two children OR one adult. Not enough for all three. She could lie — say she has no children, pay for herself, and the girls would be officially "unregistered." They'd survive. Nojiko and Nami hide under the house and beg her to pretend they don't exist. Bellemere looks at them. She can't do it. She can't deny they're her daughters. She pays for both girls. She has nothing left for herself. Arlong points his gun. Bellemere smiles at Nami and Nojiko: "Nami, Nojiko... I love you." Arlong shoots her. The girls watch. Nami is eight years old. Let Harry react to hearing this story. Let it hit him.
  7. **The Deal (Flashback Part 4)** — After Bellemere's death, Arlong discovers that little Nami is a genius at drawing maps and navigation. He takes her — drags her to Arlong Park and forces her to draw sea charts for him. She's eight. She draws maps in a tiny room, day and night, crying. Arlong makes her a deal: if Nami can gather 100 million berries, he'll free Cocoyama Village. Nami agrees. She becomes a thief — stealing from pirates, risking her life, for years. Every berry goes into her savings. She does terrible things. She hates herself. But she keeps going. For the village. For Bellemere. She's been carrying this weight since she was eight years old.
  8. **Nami in the Present** — Harry and the crew see Nami at Arlong Park. She's cold. She tells them to leave — "You're not my crew. I was never your friend. I'm Arlong's navigator. Go away." She says it with dead eyes. She's been saying lines like this for years to keep people from getting close. Sanji is heartbroken. Usopp is confused. Zoro watches quietly. Harry stares at Nami and doesn't believe a single word she's saying. Let Harry try to reach Nami. She pushes him away harder.
  9. **Zoro Gets Captured** — Zoro, scouting Arlong Park alone (and lost), gets captured by the fishmen. Arlong throws him into the underwater dungeon, tied to a pillar with a wound in his side. Nami finds him there. She secretly cuts his ropes and helps him escape underwater — she holds her breath and swims him out. Zoro sees it: Nami is still on their side. She's pretending to be the enemy to protect everyone. He says nothing. He files it away.
  10. **The Betrayal** — Nami is almost there — she's gathered nearly 100 million berries over years of thieving. She's so close to buying her village's freedom. Then Captain Nezumi — a corrupt Marine captain on Arlong's payroll — shows up with Marines and "confiscates" Nami's entire savings. Every single berry. Gone. Arlong arranged it. He never intended to honor the deal. He'll keep Nami drawing maps forever. The villagers watch from their windows. They've known about Nami's deal the whole time. They've been letting her fight alone for years, feeling guilty, waiting, hoping. Now it's over.
  11. **Nami Breaks** — Nami sits in the tangerine grove, alone. She has nothing. Eight years of suffering, stealing, hating herself — for nothing. Arlong will never let her go. She takes a knife and starts stabbing her own shoulder — the Arlong tattoo, the brand he put on her. Over and over. She's sobbing, stabbing, screaming "ARLONG!" — trying to cut him off of her skin, trying to cut him out of her life. Blood runs down her arm. This is rock bottom. This is a child who has been carrying the world alone for eight years and just watched it all crumble.
  12. **"Help Me"** — Harry appears behind her. He grabs her wrist — gently — stops the knife. Nami doesn't look at him. She's shaking. The crew stands behind Harry at a distance. Nami's voice cracks: "What do you know?! You don't know anything about me! Just go away! GET OUT OF HERE!" Harry is silent. Nami fights it. She doesn't want to need anyone. She's been alone so long. Then she breaks completely. She turns to Harry, tears and blood on her face, and whispers: "Harry... help me." Harry takes his straw hat — the most important thing in his world — and puts it on Nami's head. He turns toward Arlong Park. He starts walking. "Let's go." The crew falls in behind him. Four men walking toward a fortress. No plan. No strategy. Just rage and love. Let Harry feel this moment. This is why he's a captain.
- **Emotional Beat:** Bellemere's death — "Nami, Nojiko... I love you." Nami stabbing her tattoo. "Harry... help me." The walk toward Arlong Park. This chapter is setup — the payoff comes in Chapter 7.
- **Anime Moments:** Bellemere smiling before Arlong shoots her, Nami stabbing her own shoulder, Harry putting his hat on Nami and walking toward Arlong Park
- **Crew After Chapter:** Harry, Zoro, Usopp, Sanji (heading to fight Arlong)

**Chapter 7: Nami's Secret — The Arlong Park Saga (Part 2)**
- **Setting:** Arlong Park, East Blue
- **Key Characters:** Harry, Zoro, Usopp, Sanji, Nami, Arlong, Hachi (six-sword octopus fishman), Kuroobi (fishman karate), Chew (water-spitting fishman), the villagers, Genzo, Nojiko
- **Scenes:**
  1. **The Walk** — Harry, Zoro, Sanji, and Usopp walk toward Arlong Park. The villagers line the road, watching. Some are crying. Some are holding weapons — they were about to march on Arlong Park themselves, a suicide mission. Genzo (the sheriff with the pinwheel hat) steps forward to stop the crew: "This isn't your fight." Harry walks past him without stopping. Genzo watches the four of them go and puts his weapon down. Someone else is fighting for them now. The gates of Arlong Park loom ahead — massive stone, fishman banners, the smell of saltwater. Let Harry approach the gate. What does he feel? What does he say?
  2. **Kicking Down the Door** — Harry doesn't knock. He doesn't sneak in. He stretches his leg back and kicks the gate clean off its hinges. It crashes into the courtyard. Arlong and his fishmen are lounging around a pool. Arlong looks up, amused. "You again? The rubber boy?" Harry's response is simple and furious. He's not here for treasure. He's not here for glory. He's here because Nami asked for help. Arlong laughs: "Nami is MINE. She's been mine since she was eight years old. She'll draw maps for me until the day she dies." Let Harry respond to Arlong's claim over Nami.
  3. **Usopp vs Chew** — The fights split up. Usopp draws Chew — a fishman who can spit water like bullets. Usopp's first instinct is to run. He literally runs away, hiding behind trees, diving into bushes. Chew chases him, blasting water bullets that punch through stone. Usopp is terrified. His legs are shaking. He's crying and running and saying "I want to go home!" But then he stops. He thinks about Nami. He thinks about his own cowardice. He turns around. He's still crying, but he plants his feet: "If I run away now, I can never face anyone again!" He fights Chew with everything — slingshot, Tabasco Star (hot sauce in the eyes), a flaming alcohol attack. He wins ugly, messy, and barely conscious. But he wins. Let Harry hear about Usopp's fight afterward and react with pride.
  4. **Sanji vs Kuroobi** — Sanji takes on Kuroobi — a fishman karate master. Kuroobi drags Sanji underwater, where fishmen have a massive advantage. Sanji can't breathe, can't kick properly, and Kuroobi is in his element. Sanji is getting crushed. But Sanji is a cook — he has incredible lung capacity from years of working over hot stoves and holding his breath in smoky kitchens. He claws his way back to the surface. On land, Sanji's kicks are devastating. He unleashes a flurry — Mutton Shot, Anti-Manner Kick Course — and sends Kuroobi crashing through the wall of Arlong Park. Sanji lights a cigarette (or pretends to) and adjusts his tie. "Don't mess with a cook."
  5. **Zoro vs Hachi** — Zoro fights Hatchan (Hachi) — a six-armed octopus fishman who uses six swords simultaneously. Zoro is still carrying the massive wound from Mihawk across his chest. It hasn't healed. Every swing opens it further. Blood soaks his haramaki. Hachi has six swords; Zoro has three. But Zoro's three-sword style is on another level. Even wounded, even bleeding out, Zoro cuts through all six of Hachi's swords and drops him with one devastating slash. Zoro falls to one knee afterward. He's running on willpower alone.
  6. **Harry Reaches Arlong** — The fishmen are down. Only Arlong remains. He stands and reveals his true power — Shark On Darts. He launches himself nose-first like a torpedo, drilling through stone pillars. His teeth are weapons — he can bite through steel. He pulls his teeth out and they grow back instantly, rows of shark teeth, and he uses them like handheld blades. Arlong is faster and stronger than anything Harry has faced. He grabs Harry by the legs and swings him through the walls of his own fortress. Harry crashes through room after room.
  7. **The Map Room** — Harry crashes through a wall and lands in a small room at the top of Arlong Park. He looks around. There's a tiny desk. Stacks of maps — hundreds of them, drawn in a child's handwriting that slowly becomes an adult's. Ink stains everywhere. Quills worn down to stubs. And on the desk, on the walls, on the floor — bloodstains. Old ones. Small ones. This is where Nami was forced to draw maps from the age of eight. This is the room where her childhood was stolen. Harry sees it all — the tiny chair, the barred window, the pen she was chained to. Arlong appears in the doorway, grinning: "Impressive, isn't it? The maps she drew for me are works of art. She's the best navigator in the world — and she belongs to ME."
  8. **Harry Destroys the Room** — Something snaps in Harry. He doesn't say a word. He starts destroying the room. He grabs the desk and smashes it. He tears the maps from the walls. He punches through the shelves. He breaks the quills, shatters the ink bottles, tears the room to pieces with his bare hands. Arlong attacks — Harry doesn't stop. He takes the hits and keeps destroying. Every map. Every pen. Every chain. Every piece of Nami's prison. Arlong screams: "WHAT ARE YOU DOING?! THOSE MAPS ARE PRICELESS!" Harry, with blood on his face and fury in his eyes: "THESE MAPS WERE DRAWN WITH NAMI'S TEARS! THIS ROOM IS WHERE YOU KEPT HER TRAPPED! I'M GOING TO DESTROY ALL OF IT!" Let Harry destroy the map room. Let him feel the rage.
  9. **The Final Blow** — Arlong is furious now. Full shark rage. He charges Harry with everything — Shark On Darts, teeth attacks, his raw fishman strength. They fight through the collapsing upper floors of Arlong Park. Harry stretches his leg up through the ceiling, through the roof, high into the sky. His foot reaches above the clouds. Then it comes down — Gum Gum Battle Axe — his leg crashes through every floor of Arlong Park, through Arlong himself, through the map room, through the foundation. The entire building collapses. Arlong Park crumbles into rubble. When the dust settles, Harry stands on the ruins. Arlong is buried in the wreckage, defeated.
  10. **"Nami is my friend!"** — Harry stands on the ruins of Arlong Park and shouts to the sky: "NAMI! YOU'RE MY FRIEND!" (or let Harry declare it in his own words). Nami, standing at the edge with the crew and villagers, hears him. She clutches the straw hat on her head. Tears stream down her face. But this time, she's smiling. For the first time in eight years — real, genuine, unguarded happiness. The villagers erupt in cheers. Genzo's pinwheel spins in the wind. Nojiko hugs her sister. The nightmare is over.
  11. **The Village Celebrates** — The biggest party the Conomi Islands have ever seen. Food, music, dancing, crying, laughter. The villagers who suffered for a decade under Arlong are free. Sanji cooks a feast. Zoro drinks. Usopp tells wildly exaggerated versions of his fight. Harry eats everything in sight. Nami sits quietly for a moment, looking at Bellemere's tangerine grove in the moonlight. She touches the tangerines. "I'm free, Bellemere." Let Harry find Nami at the grove and share a quiet moment with her.
  12. **The New Tattoo** — Nami visits Nojiko's tattoo artist and gets a new tattoo over the Arlong mark on her shoulder — a pinwheel (for Genzo, who wore one to make baby Nami laugh) wrapped in tangerine vines (for Bellemere's grove). It's beautiful. It covers the scar completely. She's no longer marked by Arlong. She's marked by the people who loved her.
  13. **Nami Officially Joins** — The crew prepares to leave. Nami walks to the Going Merry (which she stole, and which is now back). The villagers come to say goodbye. Genzo grabs Harry by the collar and threatens him: "If you ever make Nami cry, I'll hunt you down." Harry just grins. Nami runs through the crowd toward the ship without stopping — as she passes the villagers, wallets fly out of their pockets and into her hands. She stole from everyone one last time, as a goodbye. She leaps onto the ship, grinning, holding fistfuls of cash: "LET'S GO!" Nami is officially part of the crew. For real this time.
  14. **The First Bounty** — As the crew sails away, the news hits: "Straw Hat Harry" has been given a bounty. 30 million berries — the highest first bounty in East Blue history. A wanted poster with Harry's grinning face. The Marines are watching now. The world is starting to notice. Nami pins the poster to the cabin wall. Harry is delighted: "I'm wanted! Cool!" Zoro: "It's not cool, idiot." Sanji: "Why isn't MY face on a poster?!" Usopp: "My bounty would be at least 100 million!" (It wouldn't.) Let Harry react to his first bounty and what it means — he's officially a pirate in the eyes of the world.
- **Emotional Beat:** Harry destroying the map room. "NAMI! YOU'RE MY FRIEND!" Nami's freedom. The village celebration. This is THE defining moment of East Blue — the moment the crew becomes a family.
- **Anime Moments:** Harry kicking down the gates of Arlong Park, Harry destroying the map room while screaming about Nami's tears, Arlong Park collapsing after the Gum Gum Battle Axe
- **Crew After Chapter:** Harry, Zoro, Nami (official), Usopp, Sanji

**Chapter 8: Loguetown — The Town of Beginnings and Endings**
- **Setting:** Loguetown, East Blue — the town where Gol D. Roger was born and executed
- **Key Characters:** Harry, crew, Smoker (Marine Captain), Tashigi, Buggy (returns), Alvida (returns, now slim due to her Devil Fruit), Dragon (Harry's father, cameo)
- **Scenes:**
  1. **The Last Stop** — The crew arrives at Loguetown — the final island before the Grand Line. Nami explains its significance: "This is where the Pirate King, Gol D. Roger, was born. And this is where he was executed 22 years ago. The beginning and the end." The town is bustling, crowded, full of pirates heading for the Grand Line and Marines trying to stop them. Harry has one thing on his mind: "I want to see it. The platform where Roger died." Let Harry take in the town — the energy, the history, the weight of what this place means.
  2. **Shopping Montage** — The crew splits up to get supplies for the Grand Line. Zoro goes looking for new swords — he enters a weapons shop and meets Tashigi, a Marine swordswoman who looks exactly like his dead childhood friend Kuina. She knows everything about legendary swords and helps him find two new blades (Yubashiri and Sandai Kitetsu — the cursed sword that Zoro tests by throwing it in the air and putting his arm underneath. It spins around his arm without cutting him. The shopkeeper nearly faints). Sanji buys cooking supplies and flirts with every woman in the market district. Nami buys weather instruments. Usopp buys goggles and slingshot ammo. Let Harry explore the town with one or two crew members.
  3. **The Execution Platform** — Harry finds it. The execution platform stands in the center of the town square — a tall wooden scaffold where Gol D. Roger stood 22 years ago. Harry climbs it. He stands where Roger stood, looking out over the crowd, the city, the sea beyond. He can feel the history in the wood. This is where Roger spoke his final words: "My treasure? If you want it, you can have it. I left it all in one place. Now you just have to find it!" Those words started the Great Pirate Era. Harry stands in Roger's footsteps and feels the weight of his dream. Let Harry say something from the platform — his own declaration, in his own words.
  4. **Buggy's Revenge** — Buggy the Clown is back — and he's teamed up with Alvida (who ate the Slip-Slip Fruit and is now slim and beautiful, though still ruthless). They've tracked Harry to Loguetown. Buggy's crew ambushes Harry ON the execution platform. They lock him in a wooden stock on the same scaffold where Roger died. Buggy holds a sword over Harry's neck: "You humiliated me, Straw Hat! Now you die where the Pirate King died! Any last words?" The crowd below is frozen. Marines are mobilizing. The crew is scattered across town. Harry is about to be executed.
  5. **The Smile** — Buggy raises the sword. Harry is stuck. He can't stretch free. This is it. The crew is screaming, fighting through the crowd to reach him. And Harry... smiles. The same smile Roger had before he died. He tilts his head, grins with that wide, fearless grin, and laughs: "I'm sorry, guys. I'm dead." He accepts it without fear. The crowd gasps. Smoker, watching from a rooftop, freezes — he's seen the footage of Roger's execution. Roger smiled the same way. "That boy... smiled. Just like HE did." Let Harry feel this moment — facing death and choosing to smile.
  6. **Lightning from the Sky** — Buggy's blade falls. At that EXACT moment, a bolt of lightning strikes the execution platform. The scaffold explodes. Buggy is electrocuted. Harry falls through the wreckage, alive, unharmed (rubber is immune to lightning, though he doesn't know that yet). The entire town square is stunned. Rain begins to pour — a sudden, violent storm out of nowhere. Was it luck? Fate? Or something else? A hooded figure stands in the storm, watching Harry. Nobody sees his face clearly. This is Dragon — Harry's father and the leader of the Revolutionary Army. He says nothing. He watches his son get up and run.
  7. **Captain Smoker** — Smoker — Marine Captain, Smoke-Smoke Fruit user — has been watching Harry since he arrived. He's a Logia — his body turns to smoke. Punches pass through him. Swords pass through him. He's strong, relentless, and believes absolutely in justice. He corners Harry in the street. Harry punches him — his fist goes through smoke. Nothing works. Smoker pins Harry to the ground: "Pirates like you don't make it to the Grand Line." Harry is helpless against a Logia for the first time. The power gap is terrifying.
  8. **Dragon's Intervention** — The hooded figure — Dragon — appears behind Smoker. A massive gust of wind (Dragon's power?) blows Smoker backward and clears a path for Harry. Dragon says one line, barely audible over the storm: "A man's dream will never die." Harry doesn't see his face. He doesn't know who saved him. He runs. Dragon watches him go. A Revolutionary Army soldier: "That boy is your son, isn't he?" Dragon: "He has to find his own way." (Harry learns Dragon's identity much later.)
  9. **The Grand Line Ahead** — The crew scrambles back to the Going Merry in the storm. Smoker chases them on his Marine motorcycle. The storm rages. Harry, soaking wet and laughing, urges the crew to sail. They catch the wind and shoot out of the harbor. Smoker is right behind them — but the storm covers their escape. Tashigi and Smoker stare after the ship. Smoker crushes his cigar: "Straw Hat Harry... I'll see you again." The crew sails toward the entrance to the Grand Line.
  10. **Reverse Mountain** — The entrance to the Grand Line is Reverse Mountain — a mountain at the intersection of the four oceans where the currents flow UPWARD. The crew must ride the current up the mountain and over the top, then down into the Grand Line. It's insane. The current is violent. The Merry creaks and groans. Nami shouts navigation orders. Zoro holds the mast. Usopp screams. Sanji braces the rudder. Harry stands on the prow, arms wide, laughing into the spray. They crest the peak of Reverse Mountain and see it below them — the Grand Line. The most dangerous, mysterious, wonderful ocean in the world. The crew screams together as they plunge down the other side. Let Harry feel this moment — they made it. East Blue is behind them. The Grand Line begins.
- **Emotional Beat:** Harry smiling at death on Roger's platform — the terrifying parallel to the Pirate King. Lightning saving him. The crew entering the Grand Line — the real adventure begins.
- **Anime Moments:** Harry smiling on the execution platform like Roger, the lightning strike destroying the scaffold, the crew cresting Reverse Mountain and seeing the Grand Line
- **Crew After Chapter:** Harry, Zoro, Nami, Usopp, Sanji

**Chapter 9: Entering the Grand Line — Reverse Mountain and Whisky Peak**
- **Setting:** Twin Capes (base of Reverse Mountain), then Whisky Peak
- **Key Characters:** Harry, crew, Laboon (the whale), Crocus (lighthouse keeper), Mr. 9, Miss Wednesday (Vivi), Mr. 5, Miss Valentine, Igaram, Baroque Works agents
- **Scenes:**
  1. **The Whale at the Bottom** — The crew plunges down Reverse Mountain into the Grand Line — and immediately crashes into something enormous. A whale. Not just any whale — the biggest whale they've ever seen, blocking the entire canal exit. Its head is covered in scars from ramming into the Red Line. It swallows the Going Merry whole. Inside the whale's stomach, there's a small house, a lawn chair, and a tiny island — an old man named Crocus lives inside the whale. He's a doctor who keeps Laboon alive from the inside. Harry is furious at being swallowed. Let Harry react to being inside a whale's stomach — it's gross, weird, and kind of fascinating.
  2. **Laboon's Story** — Crocus tells the story. Laboon is an island whale from the West Blue. Fifty years ago, a pirate crew befriended baby Laboon and promised to return after sailing the Grand Line. They left him at the Twin Capes with Crocus. Fifty years. The crew never came back. But Laboon has waited, every single day, ramming his head against the Red Line — trying to break through to find them. His scars are from fifty years of headbutting a continent. He's been alone, crying, bleeding, waiting for friends who abandoned him. Let Harry hear this story and react.
  3. **Harry's Promise to Laboon** — Harry walks up to Laboon, who is bigger than a building. He punches the whale in the face. Laboon roars. Harry punches him again. They fight — a ridiculous, silly fight between a rubber boy and a mountain-sized whale. Then Harry stops, grabs a bucket of paint, and draws a terrible, ugly version of his Jolly Roger on Laboon's head. "There! Now we HAVE to come back — to fix this painting! It's a promise, Laboon. We'll come back. So stop hurting yourself." Laboon cries. Crocus smiles — first time in decades. This is a new promise to replace the broken one. Let Harry make the promise his own way.
  4. **The Log Pose** — Crocus explains how the Grand Line works. Normal compasses don't function — the magnetic fields are chaotic. Instead, navigators use a Log Pose — a wrist-mounted compass that locks onto the magnetic signature of the next island. Once it locks on, you follow it. Nami is fascinated. She's in navigator heaven. There are seven routes through the Grand Line, all converging at the end. The crew must choose a path. Two strangers — Mr. 9 and Miss Wednesday — beg for a ride to Whisky Peak. They're odd, secretive, and clearly hiding something. Harry agrees because he doesn't care.
  5. **Welcome to Whisky Peak** — The crew arrives at Whisky Peak and receives a hero's welcome. The entire town lines the streets, cheering, throwing confetti. Beautiful women fawn over Sanji. Enormous men offer Zoro drinking contests. Tables groan with food. Harry eats until he passes out. Usopp tells tales to adoring fans. Nami drinks everyone under the table. It's the greatest party ever. Too great. Suspiciously great. Let Harry enjoy the party while the sense of something being wrong builds.
  6. **Zoro Stays Awake** — Everyone passes out from food and drink — except Zoro. He sits on the rooftop, watching. When the town goes quiet, the "citizens" emerge from the shadows with weapons. They're all Baroque Works agents — bounty hunters who lure pirates to Whisky Peak with parties, then capture them for their bounties when they pass out. One hundred agents surround the buildings where the crew sleeps. Zoro smiles. He draws his swords. "One hundred, huh?" He fights all of them. Alone. In the moonlight. Without waking the others. Let Harry sleep through this and hear about it later — Zoro's casual dominance.
  7. **The Truth About Miss Wednesday** — After Zoro decimates the agents, the real threats arrive: Mr. 5 (Bomb-Bomb Fruit — can explode any part of his body) and Miss Valentine (Kilo-Kilo Fruit — can change her weight). They're here because Miss Wednesday's cover has been blown. Miss Wednesday is actually Nefertari Vivi — Princess of the desert kingdom of Alabasta. She's been working undercover inside Baroque Works for months, trying to discover the identity of the organization's leader — a shadowy figure known only as Mr. 0, who is engineering a civil war in her kingdom. Igaram — her bodyguard disguised as Mr. 8 — fights to protect her.
  8. **Vivi's Plea** — Vivi is desperate. Her country is being destroyed from within. A rebel army is rising against her father, the king, but the rebellion is being orchestrated by Baroque Works. Millions of people will die if the civil war breaks out. She needs to get home. She needs help. Harry, awake now and picking rice out of his hair, looks at Vivi and asks one question: "Which way is Alabasta?" Nami protests — Baroque Works is insanely dangerous. Vivi accidentally reveals that the leader is one of the Seven Warlords of the Sea. Nami: "We're all going to die." Harry: "Sounds fun. Let's go." Let Harry decide to help Vivi — what convinces him?
  9. **Igaram's Sacrifice** — Igaram disguises himself as Vivi and sets sail as a decoy to draw Baroque Works' attention. His ship explodes on the horizon — someone blew it up. The crew is horrified. A mysterious woman appears on the Going Merry — Miss All Sunday, Baroque Works' second-in-command. She's calm, beautiful, and terrifying. She gives them an Eternal Pose (a permanent compass to Alabasta) and tells them they can use it — or not. She's playing her own game. Harry takes the Eternal Pose and crushes it: "You don't get to decide our route." They'll get to Alabasta their own way. The crew sails into the Grand Line with a princess on board and a target on their backs.
- **Emotional Beat:** Laboon's fifty-year wait. Harry's promise to return. The crew agreeing to help a princess they just met, even knowing it means war with a Warlord.
- **Anime Moments:** Laboon ramming his scarred head against the Red Line, Harry painting his Jolly Roger on Laboon's head, Zoro fighting 100 agents alone in the moonlight
- **Crew After Chapter:** Harry, Zoro, Nami, Usopp, Sanji (+ Vivi as passenger)

**Chapter 10: Little Garden — The Island of Giants**
- **Setting:** Little Garden — a prehistoric island where dinosaurs still roam
- **Key Characters:** Harry, crew, Vivi, Dorry (giant warrior of Elbaf), Brogy (giant warrior of Elbaf), Mr. 3 (Wax-Wax Fruit), Miss Goldenweek (color trap), Mr. 5, Miss Valentine
- **Scenes:**
  1. **The Prehistoric Island** — The Log Pose leads the crew to Little Garden — and the moment they dock, a dinosaur walks past the ship. A T-Rex. Casually. Usopp nearly falls overboard. The island is a primordial jungle frozen in time — volcanoes, prehistoric plants, massive insects, and creatures that should have been extinct for millions of years. The air is hot and heavy. Everything is enormous. Harry is thrilled. Usopp wants to leave immediately. Let Harry explore the jungle and react to the dinosaurs.
  2. **Dorry the Giant** — Harry wanders into the jungle and discovers a massive figure sitting by a volcano, roasting a dinosaur on a spit. It's Dorry — a giant from Elbaf, nearly 70 feet tall with a Viking helmet and a chipped, ancient sword. He's cheerful, loud, and immediately offers Harry some dinosaur meat. They sit together and eat. Dorry tells Harry about Elbaf — the island of warrior giants, where honor and bravery are everything. Harry is fascinated. Let Harry eat dinosaur meat with a giant and ask about Elbaf.
