  3. **Brogy the Giant** — Meanwhile, on the other side of the island, Usopp stumbles into Brogy — the other giant. Brogy is similarly enormous, with a different Viking style and a huge axe. He's just as friendly. Usopp is terrified at first but quickly becomes captivated by Brogy's stories of Elbaf warriors. Brogy treats Usopp like a fellow warrior. Usopp puffs up with pride. Something awakens in Usopp — the dream of being a brave warrior, like the giants of Elbaf.
  4. **The 100-Year Duel** — A volcano erupts — that's the signal. Dorry and Brogy stand, face each other across the island, and charge. They fight with everything they have — sword against axe, two giants clashing with force that shakes the earth. It's beautiful and terrifying. When it's over, it's a draw. Again. They've been fighting this same duel for over 100 years. Neither remembers what started it — something about a hunting contest, who caught the bigger fish. But the fight itself is sacred. It's about honor, about proving themselves to each other, about a friendship so deep it can only be expressed through combat. Usopp watches with tears in his eyes: "THIS is what warriors are." Let Harry and the crew witness the duel and react.
  5. **Sabotage** — Mr. 3 and his partner Miss Goldenweek have been hiding on the island. Mr. 3 (Wax-Wax Fruit — creates wax that hardens like steel) sabotages the duel by putting explosives in the giants' drinks. Dorry's ale explodes in his stomach during the next duel. He falls. Brogy wins, but he knows something is wrong — Dorry would never fall from a fair blow. The honor of the duel has been violated. Brogy is devastated. Mr. 3 reveals himself and traps the weakened Dorry in a wax cage.
  6. **The Wax Trap** — Mr. 3 creates his masterpiece — a giant candelabra of wax. Nami, Vivi, and Zoro are caught in it, slowly being covered in hardening wax that will turn them into statues. The wax drips and solidifies. They're being encased alive. Zoro grabs his sword and starts cutting at his own legs, trying to free himself — he'd rather lose his legs than die trapped. The others scream at him to stop. Usopp arrives and realizes he has to do something.
  7. **Usopp's Fire Star** — Usopp, shaking with fear, steps up. Mr. 3's wax is strong — but it's still wax. Wax melts. Usopp loads a Fire Star into his slingshot and shoots at the base of the candelabra. The wax catches fire. Harry arrives and smashes through the melting wax to free the crew. Mr. 3 tries to fight back, but Harry stretches his arm and delivers a Gum Gum Bazooka that sends the wax man flying. Miss Goldenweek's color traps (paint that controls emotions) nearly stop Harry — she paints "relaxation" on him and he sits down to have tea mid-battle. Usopp burns the paint off him. Let Harry deal with Miss Goldenweek's weird powers.
  8. **The Giants' Farewell** — With Mr. 3 defeated, Dorry and Brogy stand together for the first time in 100 years — as allies rather than opponents. The crew needs to leave, but a massive Sea King-infested current blocks the way. The two giants stand at the shore, raise their weapons, and deliver a combined attack — a single, devastating simultaneous slash that splits the sea and kills the Sea King. The path opens. It's the most powerful display of strength the crew has ever seen. Brogy to the crew: "Go with the pride of Elbaf warriors behind you!" Let Harry thank the giants. Usopp declares his dream: "I'm going to visit Elbaf someday and become a brave warrior of the sea!"
- **Emotional Beat:** The giants' 100-year duel — honor and friendship that transcends time. Zoro willing to cut off his own legs rather than die trapped. Usopp's dream of Elbaf is born.
- **Anime Moments:** Dorry and Brogy clashing in their 100-year duel, Zoro trying to cut his own legs free, the giants' combined attack splitting the sea
- **Crew After Chapter:** Harry, Zoro, Nami, Usopp, Sanji (+ Vivi)

**Chapter 11: Drum Island — The Doctor with the Blue Nose**
- **Setting:** Drum Island — a winter island with massive drum-shaped mountains
- **Key Characters:** Harry, crew, Vivi, Tony Tony Chopper, Dr. Kureha, Dr. Hiriluk (flashback), Wapol (former king), Dalton, Kureha
- **Scenes:**
  1. **Nami Falls Ill** — On the ocean between islands, Nami collapses. High fever, shaking, barely conscious. She's burning up. The crew panics — no one knows medicine. Vivi presses a cold cloth to Nami's forehead. Sanji is beside himself with worry. Harry stands over Nami, fists clenched. They need a doctor. Now. Vivi knows of a winter island nearby with a famous doctor. The crew changes course immediately. Let Harry decide how to handle the crisis — does he stay with Nami or take the helm?
  2. **The Frozen Kingdom** — Drum Island. Snow everywhere. The mountains are shaped like drums — flat-topped cylinders of rock rising thousands of feet into the sky. The tallest one has a castle perched on top. The people are scared and suspicious. They reveal the truth: the former king, Wapol, exiled or killed every doctor on the island before he fled from pirates. There is only ONE doctor left — a witch called Dr. Kureha, who lives in the castle at the very top of the tallest drum mountain. There is no path. No road. Just sheer, frozen cliff faces.
  3. **Climbing the Mountain** — Harry puts Nami on his back and starts climbing. Sanji follows. The mountain is nearly vertical — thousands of feet of frozen rock in a blizzard. Harry climbs with his bare hands, rubber fingers gripping ice. Nami burns against his back with fever. The cold is brutal. Sanji fights off Lapahn (giant rabbits, aggressive and territorial) on the mountain slopes. An avalanche nearly kills them. Sanji breaks his spine protecting Nami from falling rocks. Harry carries BOTH of them — Nami on his back, Sanji under his arm — and keeps climbing. His hands bleed. His fingers crack. He climbs with his teeth when his hands give out. Let Harry push through the pain — why does he keep climbing?
  4. **The Castle at the Top** — Harry reaches the summit, half-dead, frozen, bleeding. He collapses on the castle doorstep. A small figure peers out from behind a doorframe — a reindeer standing on two legs, wearing a pink hat, with a blue nose. It screams and runs away. An old woman appears — Dr. Kureha. She's 139 years old and looks 60. She's terrifying, brilliant, and immediately starts treating Nami and Sanji. She whips Harry with a cane for tracking blood on her floor. Harry passes out from exhaustion. He climbed a 5,000-foot frozen mountain carrying two people. Let Harry wake up in the castle and take in his surroundings.
  5. **The Reindeer Doctor** — Harry wakes up and meets Chopper properly. Tony Tony Chopper is a reindeer who ate the Human-Human Fruit (Hito Hito no Mi). He can talk, walk upright, think like a human, and transform between three forms (reindeer, human hybrid, and a small tanuki-like form). He's Dr. Kureha's assistant and a brilliant doctor despite being young. He's also deeply shy — when Harry compliments him, Chopper does a wiggly dance and shouts "Shut up! Compliments don't make me happy, you jerk!" (He's clearly delighted.) But Chopper is terrified of people. He hides behind doors the wrong way. He won't come close. Let Harry try to befriend Chopper — talk to him, share food, make him laugh.
  6. **The Blue Nose (Flashback Part 1)** — Chopper's backstory begins. He was born a normal reindeer — except for his blue nose. The other reindeer in the herd rejected him for being different. When he ate the Human-Human Fruit and gained the ability to walk and talk, both the reindeer and the humans rejected him — too human for animals, too animal for humans. He was completely alone. He wandered the snowy mountains, cold and starving, a monster to everyone. Let Harry hear this and react — does it remind him of anyone else who was different?
  7. **Dr. Hiriluk (Flashback Part 2)** — One man took Chopper in. Dr. Hiriluk — a quack doctor with a skull-and-crossbones flag, terrible medicine, and the biggest heart on the island. He found Chopper bleeding in the snow and brought him home. Chopper bit him, kicked him, tried to run. Hiriluk stayed. He bandaged Chopper's wounds. He gave him the pink hat. He called him "son." For the first time in Chopper's life, someone wanted him around. They lived together in a tiny cabin, Hiriluk teaching Chopper about medicine (badly) and about his dream: to cure the sick hearts of Drum Island's people by making cherry blossoms bloom in the winter.
  8. **The Poison Mushroom (Flashback Part 3)** — Hiriluk was dying. A terminal illness. He hid it from Chopper but Chopper found out. Desperate, Chopper searched the entire island for a legendary healing mushroom — a mushroom with a skull-and-crossbones symbol that Hiriluk's medical book said could cure any disease. Chopper fought through blizzards, fell off cliffs, was attacked by animals. He came back broken and bleeding, holding the mushroom triumphantly. Hiriluk cried — and ate it. But the skull-and-crossbones symbol meant it was POISON. Chopper didn't know. He was a reindeer reading a medical book. Hiriluk ate it anyway, knowing it would kill him faster, because he couldn't bear to reject Chopper's love. Let this sink in. Let Harry feel it.
  9. **Hiriluk's Death (Flashback Part 4)** — Hiriluk knows he's dying now — faster, because of the poison. Wapol has trapped the island's remaining doctors at his castle as bait, pretending they're sick. Hiriluk walks into the trap willingly. He stands before Wapol and the doctors. He knows it's a trap. He doesn't care. He gives one final speech: "When do you think people die? When they're shot through the heart with a bullet? No. When they have an incurable disease? No. When they drink poison soup? No! A man dies when he is FORGOTTEN! I will not die, partner. Because my dream... my dream will live on!" He drinks a vial and blows himself up — dying on his own terms, with his flag flying. Chopper, watching from the distance, screams into the snow. This is why Chopper became a doctor. To cure everything. To make sure no one dies like Hiriluk did.
  10. **Wapol Returns** — In the present, Wapol — the former king, a fat tyrant who ate the Munch-Munch Fruit (he can eat anything and absorb it into his body) — returns to Drum Island with his army to reclaim his kingdom. He heads for the castle. He insults Hiriluk's flag, which still flies from the tower. Chopper is furious — that flag represents his father's dream. Harry is furious too. Let Harry decide to fight Wapol. This is personal — Wapol is the reason this island suffered.
  11. **Harry vs Wapol** — Wapol eats cannons and becomes a cannon-man. He eats his own subordinates and fuses with them. He's ridiculous and dangerous. Harry fights him through the castle halls and out onto the snowy peak. Wapol tries to take down Hiriluk's flag. Harry blocks him: "Don't touch that flag!" Chopper watches — someone is protecting his father's symbol. Harry stretches his arm back as far as it will go and unleashes a Gum Gum Bazooka that sends Wapol rocketing off the mountain, over the horizon, into the sky. Wapol is launched so far he becomes a dot. The island is free.
  12. **Join My Crew** — Harry asks Chopper to be the crew's doctor. Chopper wants to come — but he's scared. He's a monster. A reindeer with a blue nose who talks. Harry stares at him: "Shut up. Let's go." (Or let Harry say it in his own words.) Chopper tries to refuse, tries to hide, tries to say no one would want a monster. Dr. Kureha kicks him (literally) toward the ship: "Get out of here, you brat! Go see the world like Hiriluk wanted!" Chopper cries and runs for the ship. Let Harry welcome Chopper aboard.
  13. **Cherry Blossom Snow** — As the Going Merry sails away from Drum Island, Dr. Kureha fulfills Hiriluk's dream. She fires his life's work — a special powder — into the sky from the castle cannons. It mixes with the falling snow. Suddenly, the snow over the entire island turns PINK. Cherry blossoms. In winter. Falling like snow across the frozen kingdom. Hiriluk's dream — cherry blossoms blooming on a winter island — has come true. Chopper stands on the deck of the Going Merry, looking back at his home, and sees it. Pink snow falling over everything. He breaks down sobbing. "Doctor... your cherry blossoms are blooming." The crew stands behind him quietly. Dalton and the islanders look up at the pink snow and cry. Let Harry stand next to Chopper and share this moment.
- **Emotional Beat:** Hiriluk's death and his speech about when people truly die. The poison mushroom — Chopper's love turned to tragedy. Cherry blossom snow. Chopper sobbing on the ship. One of the saddest and most beautiful backstories in One Piece.
- **Anime Moments:** Harry climbing the frozen mountain carrying Nami and Sanji, Hiriluk's final speech and explosion, pink cherry blossom snow falling over the island as Chopper sails away
- **Crew After Chapter:** Harry, Zoro, Nami, Usopp, Sanji, Chopper

**Chapter 12: Alabasta (Part 1) — The Desert Kingdom**
- **Setting:** Alabasta — a vast desert kingdom in civil war
- **Key Characters:** Harry, crew, Vivi, Crocodile (Mr. 0), Nico Robin (Miss All Sunday), Baroque Works officers, Pell, Chaka, the rebel army, King Cobra
- **Key Events:**
  - Arrive in Alabasta — Vivi's kingdom is tearing itself apart. A rebel army believes the king caused a drought, but it's actually Crocodile's scheme
  - Meet the Baroque Works officer agents — Mr. 1 (Daz Bones, steel body), Mr. 2 Bon Clay (shapeshifter who becomes a friend), Miss Doublefinger, etc.
  - Discover Crocodile's identity — one of the Seven Warlords of the Sea. Sand-Sand Fruit. He's been engineering the civil war to seize the ancient weapon Pluton hidden in Alabasta
  - Robin (Miss All Sunday) is Crocodile's partner — mysterious, dangerous, can read Poneglyphs
  - The crew splits up to stop the war and confront Baroque Works
  - Individual fights: Zoro vs Mr. 1 (Zoro learns to cut steel), Sanji vs Mr. 2, Nami vs Miss Doublefinger, Usopp vs Mr. 4, Chopper vs Mr. 4's partner
  - Vivi tries desperately to stop the war between the rebels and the royal army
- **Scenes:**
  1. **Crossing the Desert** — The crew arrives in Alabasta and faces the desert. Endless sand, scorching heat, no shade. Harry and Usopp are delirious within hours. Chopper is dying in his fur coat. Zoro is somehow lost in a DESERT. Sanji carries water for Nami and Vivi only. Vivi walks ahead, anxious. Dried-up riverbeds, abandoned villages. Let Harry experience the desert crossing.
  2. **The Dying Kingdom** — Towns with no water. Starving people. Angry mobs. The rebels believe King Cobra caused the drought. Vivi knows the truth: Crocodile has been using Dance Powder to frame the king. Every dead soldier is Crocodile's doing. Vivi is desperate. Let Harry see what Crocodile has done.
  3. **Mr. 2 Bon Clay — The Unexpected Friend** — Before landing, the crew meets Bon Clay. Clone-Clone Fruit — copies anyone's face by touching them. Flamboyant, dramatic, hilarious. He touches each crew member's face as a greeting, not knowing they are enemies. Harry and Bon Clay bond immediately with a friendship dance on deck. This friendship will matter later.
  4. **The X Marks** — The crew draws X marks on their left arms, hidden under bandages, to identify each other against Bon Clay's disguises. "If you see the X, it is really us." This mark becomes iconic.
  5. **Arriving in Alubarna** — The rebel army marches on the capital. The crew splits up to create diversions and fight Baroque Works agents while Vivi runs for the rebel leader Koza.
  6. **Zoro vs Mr. 1 — Cutting Steel** — Mr. 1's body turns to steel blades (Dice-Dice Fruit). Zoro's swords bounce off. Near death, Zoro closes his eyes and hears "the breath of all things." One slash. He cuts through steel. A major power-up.
  7. **Sanji vs Mr. 2 Bon Clay** — Bon Clay shifts into Nami mid-fight. Sanji freezes. He figures out the timing of the transformation and delivers a crushing kick combo. A fight of wits.
  8. **Nami vs Miss Doublefinger** — Nami's first solo fight. She uses the Clima-Tact (Usopp built it). Most attacks produce party tricks. She figures out the real power: weather manipulation. Thunderbolt Tempo — real lightning. She wins.
  9. **Usopp and Chopper vs Mr. 4 and Miss Merry Christmas** — Chaotic team fight. Miss Merry Christmas mocks Harry's dream. Usopp: "Don't DARE mock the future King of the Pirates!" Wins through teamwork and grit.
  10. **The War Begins** — Rebel army clashes with royal army. Thousands of soldiers. Vivi screams to stop but no one hears. Koza is shot by a disguised Baroque Works agent. The war has been ignited on purpose.
- **Emotional Beat:** Zoro learning to cut steel. The crew fighting alone for the first time. Vivi's futile attempt to stop the war.
- **Anime Moments:** Zoro cutting through Mr. 1's steel body, Nami summoning lightning for the first time, Usopp defending Harry's dream
- **Crew After Chapter:** Harry, Zoro, Nami, Usopp, Sanji, Chopper (plus Vivi) — scattered across Alubarna

**Chapter 13: Alabasta (Part 2) — Crocodile Falls**
- **Setting:** Alabasta — Alubarna (capital city) and the Royal Tomb
- **Key Characters:** Harry, Crocodile, Robin, Vivi
- **Key Events:**
  - Harry fights Crocodile — and LOSES. Crocodile is a Logia (sand). Harry can't touch him. Crocodile impales Harry with his hook and leaves him for dead
  - Harry survives and fights Crocodile again — discovers water makes sand solid. Fights with water-soaked fists. Loses again. Crocodile poisons him.
  - Robin saves Harry (why?)
  - Third fight — Harry uses his own blood to harden the sand. Final blow: Gum Gum Storm — a barrage of punches that sends Crocodile through solid bedrock
  - Vivi stops the war. Rain falls on Alabasta for the first time in years.
  - Vivi must choose: sail with the crew, or stay and rebuild her kingdom
  - The farewell: Vivi stands on the wall, crying, asking "Will you still call me a friend?!" The crew stands with their backs turned, raising their arms with the X marks they drew — a silent promise. No words needed.
  - Robin appears on the ship uninvited and asks to join. Harry says yes immediately.
  - Harry's new bounty: 100 million berries
- **Scenes:**
  1. **First Fight — Sand Cannot Be Touched** — Harry confronts Crocodile. Sand-Sand Fruit, a Logia. His body IS sand. Harry's Gum Gum Pistol passes through Crocodile's chest. Nothing works. Crocodile drains Harry's moisture, impales him on his golden hook, and throws him into quicksand. Harry sinks. Let Harry feel his first real defeat against a Logia — total helplessness.
  2. **Saved by Water** — Harry survives. He realizes water solidifies sand into mud. He fills his body with water and goes after Crocodile again.
  3. **Second Fight — Water Fists** — Harry soaks his fists and can land hits. But Crocodile is still vastly stronger. Ground Secco drains moisture from everything. He poisons Harry with his hook. Harry collapses. Robin finds him dying and gives him the antidote. Why? She will not say.
  4. **The Underground Tomb** — Crocodile wants Pluton — an ancient weapon hidden in Alabasta. He forces King Cobra to show the Poneglyph. Robin reads it and lies about the contents. Crocodile stabs her. Even his own partner is disposable.
  5. **Third Fight — Blood and Fury** — Harry arrives beaten twice, poisoned, running on willpower. No water left. But blood works too. Harry coats his fists in his own blood and attacks. Crocodile: "Why won't you DIE?!" Harry: "Because I made a promise to Vivi."
  6. **Gum Gum Storm** — Harry launches upward. A barrage of blood-soaked punches sends Crocodile through the tomb ceiling, through bedrock, into the sky. Water erupts from underground. Rain falls on Alabasta for the first time in years. Soldiers stop fighting. They look up. They cry.
  7. **Vivi Stops the War** — Vivi screams: "PLEASE STOP FIGHTING!" With rain falling, the soldiers hear her. The war is over. Let Harry, battered in the rubble, hear it and smile.
  8. **The Crew Recovers** — The crew gathers in the palace, all wounded, all victorious. Enormous feast. Chopper treats wounds. Sanji cooks. Harry eats 47 plates. Usopp tells exaggerated stories. A peaceful moment before the goodbye.
  9. **Vivi's Choice** — Vivi must choose: sail with the crew or stay and rebuild her kingdom. She loves them. She wants to go. But millions need their princess. She stays.
  10. **The Farewell — X Marks** — The crew sails away. Vivi runs to the palace wall, crying: "WILL YOU STILL CALL ME YOUR FRIEND?!" The crew stands with backs turned. Silently, they raise their left arms — the X marks. No words needed. Vivi raises her own X mark. Arms stay raised until neither side can see the other. One of the most iconic moments in all of One Piece.
  11. **Robin Joins** — Nico Robin is sitting on the ship, reading. "I have nowhere to go. Take responsibility." Harry: "Okay. You can join." Nami screams. Zoro does not trust her. But Harry decided.
  12. **New Bounties** — Harry: 100 million berries. Sanji's photo is a terrible sketch. Chopper gets 50 berries (they think he is a pet). The adventure in Alabasta is over.
- **Emotional Beat:** The farewell to Vivi — the X marks on their arms. Harry defeating a Warlord through sheer refusal to die. Rain falling on Alabasta.
- **Anime Moments:** Harry punching Crocodile with blood-soaked fists, Gum Gum Storm through bedrock, the crew raising X-marked arms as Vivi cries
- **Crew After Chapter:** Harry, Zoro, Nami, Usopp, Sanji, Chopper, Robin

---

### SAGA 2: SKY ISLAND (Chapters 14-17)

An island in the sky. A god who controls lightning. The crew goes where no one believes they can.

---

**Chapter 14: Jaya — The Island of Mockery**
- **Setting:** Jaya — a lawless pirate island
- **Key Characters:** Harry, crew, Bellamy (Spring-Spring Fruit), Cricket (descendant of Noland), Blackbeard (first appearance)
- **Key Events:**
  - The crew finds a galleon falling from the sky — proof that sky islands might exist. Everyone in town laughs at them.
  - Arrive at Jaya — meet Bellamy the Hyena, who mocks anyone who believes in dreams. He beats up Harry and the crew. Harry doesn't fight back — Bellamy isn't worth it (echoing Shanks's lesson about when to fight)
  - Meet Montblanc Cricket — a descendant of Noland the Liar. Noland claimed he found a city of gold 400 years ago but was executed when no one believed him. Cricket is searching the ocean floor to prove his ancestor wasn't a liar
  - Cricket helps the crew prepare to ride the Knock-Up Stream to the sky
  - Harry returns to Mock Town and defeats Bellamy with one punch
  - Brief encounter with Blackbeard (Marshall D. Teach) — he tells Harry: "A man's dream will never die!" Harry and Blackbeard agree on this without knowing they'll become enemies
  - The Knock-Up Stream launches the Going Merry into the sky
- **Scenes:**
  1. **A Ship Falls from the Sky** — The crew is sailing peacefully when a massive galleon crashes from the sky, nearly crushing the Going Merry. An ancient ship, covered in barnacles and sky creatures, falls from the clouds. Inside they find a map, strange shells called Dials, and evidence of a place above the clouds. Harry is immediately excited: "There's an island in the sky! Let's go!" Everyone else thinks he's lost his mind. Nami and Robin study the evidence. The Log Pose points upward.
  2. **Mock Town** — They arrive at Jaya — a lawless pirate island. Mock Town is rough, violent, and full of people who mock dreamers. Harry asks around about sky islands. Everyone laughs at him. "Sky islands? What are you, a kid?" The mockery is relentless. Let Harry feel what it is like to have his dream laughed at.
  3. **Bellamy the Hyena** — Bellamy is the big shot of Mock Town. Spring-Spring Fruit — his legs become springs, letting him bounce at high speed. He represents everything Harry is not: a pirate who thinks dreams are stupid. He beats Harry and Zoro bloody in a bar. Harry does not fight back. Zoro does not fight back. They sit there and take it. Nami is furious: "Why won't you fight?!" Harry: "It's not worth it." This is Shanks's lesson from Chapter 1 — some fights aren't worth having. Bellamy is not worth it.
  4. **Montblanc Cricket** — The crew finds Cricket — a diver living alone on a coast, searching the ocean floor for proof that his ancestor Noland was telling the truth. 400 years ago, Noland the Explorer found a city of gold on Jaya. When he brought the king to see it, the city was gone. Noland was executed as a liar. His family has been shamed for centuries. Cricket dives every day, risking his life, looking for gold on the sea floor. He has found some — just enough to prove it was real. Let Harry connect with Cricket's dedication to a dream everyone mocks.
  5. **Preparing for the Knock-Up Stream** — Cricket and his crew (the Saruyama Alliance — monkey-themed pirates) help prepare the Going Merry to ride the Knock-Up Stream, a massive undersea explosion that shoots water miles into the sky. It only happens at certain times in certain places. The preparation is frantic — reinforcing the ship, gathering supplies, timing the current.
  6. **One Punch** — Before leaving, Harry returns to Mock Town. Bellamy has stolen Cricket's gold — the gold Cricket spent years finding. Harry walks into the bar. Bellamy launches at him with his Spring-Spring powers, bouncing at full speed. Harry does not dodge. He punches once. One single Gum Gum Pistol. Bellamy craters into the floor, unconscious. Harry picks up Cricket's gold and walks out. No words. Let Harry deliver the punch.
  7. **Blackbeard** — Outside Mock Town, Harry bumps into a large man eating cherry pie. They argue — Harry says the pie is terrible, the man says it is delicious (or vice versa). They disagree on everything but then the man says: "A man's dream will never die!" Harry grins: "Yeah!" They part ways. This is Marshall D. Teach — Blackbeard. Harry's greatest future enemy. They agree on dreams without knowing they will try to destroy each other.
  8. **The Knock-Up Stream** — The moment arrives. The sea bulges. The Going Merry is positioned. A column of water EXPLODES from the ocean, shooting straight up into the sky at impossible speed. The ship rides the geyser up, up, up — past the clouds, past the atmosphere, into the white sea above. The crew screams — some in terror, some in joy. Harry stands on the prow, laughing, arms wide. They're flying. They're going to a sky island. Let Harry feel the rush.
- **Emotional Beat:** Harry not fighting Bellamy the first time (knowing when not to fight), then destroying him with one punch for Cricket's sake. Cricket's lifelong mission. Blackbeard's ominous first meeting.
- **Anime Moments:** Harry and Zoro sitting still while Bellamy beats them, Harry's one-punch knockout of Bellamy, the Going Merry riding the Knock-Up Stream into the sky

**Chapter 15: Skypiea (Part 1) — The Land Above the Clouds**
- **Setting:** Skypiea — an island in the sky at 10,000 meters
- **Key Characters:** Harry, crew, Conis, Pagaya, Gan Fall (Sky Knight), Enel (God), the Shandians (Wyper)
- **Key Events:**
  - The crew arrives in Skypiea — a cloud island with its own people, culture, and history
  - Meet the sky people, Conis and her father Pagaya
  - Learn about "God" Enel — a tyrant who rules Skypiea with an iron fist and claims to be God. Anyone who defies him is destroyed by lightning
  - Enel ate the Rumble-Rumble Fruit (lightning Logia) — considered one of the most powerful Devil Fruits in existence
  - The Shandians — the original inhabitants — are fighting a 400-year war to reclaim their homeland (Upper Yard), which is actually part of Jaya launched into the sky centuries ago
  - The crew enters Upper Yard — a survival game set by Enel where everyone must fight to survive
  - Individual crew battles against Enel's priests (Satori, Shura, Gedatsu, Ohm)
- **Scenes:**
  1. **The White Sea** — The crew lands on clouds. Actual clouds you can walk on (Island Clouds) and swim in (Sea Clouds). The Going Merry floats on a cloud sea. Everything is white and ethereal. Chopper, Usopp, and Harry immediately jump into the cloud sea — it is like soft cotton. They find sky fish, sky creatures, and Dials (shell-shaped devices that store and release energy, sound, light, or impact).
  2. **Heaven's Gate** — An old woman at the gate charges them to enter. Harry walks past without paying. This is now a crime in Skypiea. The entire crew is technically illegal. Let Harry realize the sky has its own laws — and he has already broken them.
  3. **Conis and the Angel Beach** — They meet Conis and her father Pagaya — kind sky people with small wings on their backs. Conis plays a harp and shows them the wonders of Skypiea: Waver boats (cloud jet-skis), Dial-powered appliances, cloud homes. Harry tries to ride a Waver and crashes into everything. Nami masters it instantly (she is a navigator genius). Let Harry enjoy the wonder of the sky island.
  4. **God Enel** — The crew learns the horrifying truth. "God" Enel rules Skypiea as a tyrant. He can hear everything on the island using Observation Haki (called "Mantra" here). He controls lightning — the Rumble-Rumble Fruit, considered one of the most powerful Devil Fruits in existence. Anyone who defies him is struck by lightning from the sky. The people live in total fear. Even mentioning resistance means death.
  5. **The Shandians** — The original inhabitants of the land — the Shandians — have been fighting for 400 years to reclaim their homeland (Upper Yard), which is actually the missing half of Jaya, launched into the sky centuries ago. Their warrior leader, Wyper, is fierce, relentless, and willing to die for his ancestors' land. The conflict between sky people and Shandians has raged for generations.
  6. **Upper Yard — The Survival Game** — Enel declares a survival game. Everyone on Upper Yard — crew, Shandians, his own priests — must fight. He predicts only five will survive. The jungle is deadly, filled with giant snakes, traps, and Enel's four priests (Satori, Shura, Gedatsu, Ohm), each with unique Dial-powered combat styles.
  7. **The Crew Splits and Fights** — The crew battles through Upper Yard. Zoro fights Ohm (sword trials with iron cloud). Sanji encounters Satori's swamp ordeal. Chopper and Nami face traps. Usopp fights despite his terror. Gan Fall — the former God of Skypiea, now a knight riding a flying horse — helps the crew. Each priest uses Dials in creative combat (Impact Dials that absorb and release force, Flame Dials, Axe Dials). Let Harry fight through the jungle and encounter the bizarre challenges of sky combat.
  8. **Robin and the Poneglyph** — Robin discovers the ruins of the Golden City of Shandora — the ancient city Noland found 400 years ago. It is here, in the sky. She finds a Poneglyph with ancient text. She reads it quietly, learning about the true history. This is what Robin lives for — the truth of the world, hidden in stone.

**Chapter 16: Skypiea (Part 2) — Rubber vs Lightning**
- **Setting:** Upper Yard, the Golden Bell
- **Key Characters:** Harry, Enel, Wyper, Robin, Gan Fall
- **Key Events:**
  - Enel's plan revealed: he wants to destroy all of Skypiea and sail to the moon (the "Fairy Vearth")
  - Enel systematically eliminates fighters — his Observation Haki (Mantra) lets him hear everything on the island
  - Robin finds the Poneglyph — ancient history connected to the Golden City of Shandora
  - Enel shocks everyone with massive lightning. Seems invincible.
  - Harry faces Enel. Enel hits him with lightning — nothing happens. Rubber doesn't conduct electricity. Harry is Enel's natural enemy.
  - Enel's face = the most iconic shocked face in anime history
  - Epic battle through the sky. Enel attaches a giant gold ball to Harry's arm. Harry uses it as a weapon.
  - Harry rings the Golden Bell with a massive punch through the clouds — the sound carries all the way down to Jaya. Cricket hears it. Noland was telling the truth. The city of gold was real — it was in the sky.
  - Skypiea is freed. The Shandians and sky people reconcile after 400 years
- **Scenes:**
  1. **Enel's Judgment** — Enel systematically eliminates fighters. His Mantra lets him hear every heartbeat on the island. He strikes from anywhere with lightning. Shandians fall. Sky people fall. His own priests fall. He predicted only five would survive and is engineering that outcome.
  2. **Enel's Plan** — He wants to destroy Skypiea and sail to the moon on a gold-powered ship. Millions will die. He does not care.
  3. **The Crew Falls** — One by one, crew members are struck down. Wyper uses the Reject Dial to stop Enel's heart. Enel restarts it with his own lightning. He is practically unkillable.
  4. **Harry vs Enel — Natural Enemy** — Enel hits Harry with 200 million volts. Harry stands there grinning. "That tickled." Enel's face — the most iconic shocked face in anime history. Rubber does not conduct electricity. Harry is the one person immune to Enel's power. Let Harry feel this moment.
  5. **The Battle in the Sky** — Enel fights with lightning, Mantra, and his golden staff. He melts gold onto Harry's right arm — a massive ball weighing hundreds of pounds. Harry is dragged down.
  6. **The Gold Weapon** — Harry turns the gold ball into a wrecking ball, swinging it with his rubber arm. The fight moves upward through the clouds toward the Golden Bell.
  7. **Ringing the Golden Bell** — Harry delivers a massive punch through the clouds, hitting the Golden Bell. BONG. The sound echoes all the way down to Jaya. Cricket hears it. He falls to his knees. His ancestor was right. The city of gold was in the sky. 400 years of shame — vindicated.
  8. **Skypiea Is Free** — Enel is defeated. The Shandians and sky people reconcile after 400 years of war. Feast on the clouds. The crew takes gold (Nami makes sure). Let Harry celebrate with the sky people.
  9. **The Descent** — The crew rides down through the clouds on a giant octopus balloon. They watch the sky island disappear. Gold, Dials, and memories of a world no one will believe they visited.
- **Emotional Beat:** Cricket hearing the bell from below the clouds. 400 years of being called liars — vindicated by a bell ringing from heaven. Harry being immune to a God.
- **Anime Moments:** Enel's iconic shocked face, Harry punching the Golden Bell with the gold-covered arm, Cricket hearing the bell from below

**Chapter 17: Return and the Davy Back Fight**
- **Setting:** The sea, Long Ring Long Land
- **Key Characters:** Harry, crew, Foxy (Silver Fox), Aokiji (Admiral)
- **Key Events:**
  - The crew returns from Skypiea with gold
  - Davy Back Fight — a pirate competition against Foxy the Silver Fox. Silly, fun, comedic arc. Crew members are wagered in games
  - Foxy has the Slow-Slow Fruit. Harry wins and the crew stays together
  - **Aokiji appears.** Admiral of the Marines. Ice-Ice Fruit. He freezes the entire ocean.
  - Aokiji knows Robin and warns the crew about her past. He freezes Robin solid. Harry is furious.
  - Harry fights Aokiji and loses completely — one of the first enemies Harry simply CANNOT beat. The power gap to the top is enormous
  - Aokiji lets them go this time — but the message is clear: the crew is not ready for the New World
- **Scenes:**
  1. **Return with Gold** — The crew crashes back into the Blue Sea loaded with Skypiea gold. They exchange some at a nearby island. The crew is rich (temporarily — Nami will manage the money with an iron fist). A relaxed, fun stretch of sailing. Crew bonding. Meals. Zoro trains. Sanji cooks. Usopp tinkers with Dials. Robin reads. Chopper studies medicine. Harry naps on the figurehead. Let Harry enjoy a peaceful moment with the crew.
  2. **Long Ring Long Land** — They arrive at a bizarre island where everything is long — long dogs, long horses, long people. The crew explores this silly place. Then they meet Foxy the Silver Fox and his crew.
  3. **The Davy Back Fight Challenge** — Foxy challenges Harry to a Davy Back Fight — an ancient pirate tradition where crews compete in games and the winner steals crew members from the loser. Harry accepts because he never backs down from a challenge (Nami is furious). The games are silly and chaotic: a boat race through a ring of obstacles, a ball game, and a captain's duel.
  4. **The Games** — Foxy has the Slow-Slow Fruit — he can shoot beams that slow anything down for 30 seconds. He cheats constantly. The crew must use teamwork and creativity to win. Chopper is briefly lost to Foxy's crew (devastating — everyone panics). They win him back. The ball game is chaotic — Zoro and Sanji fight each other as much as the enemy. Let Harry play the games and experience the comedy.
  5. **Harry vs Foxy** — The captain's duel. Foxy's Slow-Slow beams are tricky — Harry gets slowed repeatedly, then hit with accumulated attacks when the effect wears off. Harry figures out he can use a mirror to reflect the beams. He defeats Foxy with a Gum Gum Flail. The crew stays together. A fun, low-stakes arc — the last one for a while.
  6. **A Man on the Ice** — After the Davy Back Fight, the crew encounters a tall, thin man sleeping on the beach. He wears a sleep mask and a Marine uniform. He is lazy, casual, and seems harmless. Then Robin sees him and goes white. She is terrified. This is Admiral Aokiji — Kuzan. Ice-Ice Fruit. One of the three most powerful Marines in the world.
  7. **Aokiji's Warning** — Aokiji tells the crew he is "just passing through." But he singles out Robin. He knows her past: Ohara, the Buster Call, the 20-year bounty on her head. He warns the crew: "That woman will bring catastrophe to you." Robin is shaking. Aokiji looks at Harry: "Can you really protect her from what is coming?" Let Harry respond to Aokiji's warning about Robin.
  8. **Aokiji Freezes Robin** — As a demonstration of power, Aokiji touches Robin and freezes her entire body solid — encased in ice. The crew panics. Harry is furious. He attacks Aokiji. Gum Gum Pistol — Aokiji's body turns to ice and reforms. Gum Gum Gatling — passes through. Harry cannot land a single real hit. Aokiji freezes Harry's arm, then his leg. A single Ice Time finishes it — Harry is flash-frozen.
  9. **The Power Gap** — The crew barely rescues Harry and Robin by thawing them. Aokiji let them go. He could have killed all of them. This is what an Admiral is. The crew is silent on the ship that night. They are not ready. Robin stares at the ocean, alone, thinking about what Aokiji said. Her past is catching up. Something is coming. Let Harry sit with the weight of this defeat — the first enemy he simply cannot beat.
- **Emotional Beat:** The crew's first encounter with an Admiral-level threat. The terrifying realization that they are still small fish. Robin's hidden past begins to surface — foreshadowing Water 7.
- **Anime Moments:** Aokiji freezing Robin solid, Harry's rubber fist passing through Aokiji's ice body, the crew sitting in silence after the defeat

---

### SAGA 3: WATER 7 / ENIES LOBBY (Chapters 18-25)

The greatest saga in One Piece. The crew nearly breaks apart. They lose their ship. They declare war on the World Government. They save Robin. Everything changes.

---

**Chapter 18: Water 7 (Part 1) — The City on the Water**
- **Setting:** Water 7 — a beautiful city of shipwrights and canals
- **Key Characters:** Harry, crew, Iceburg, Franky, Galley-La shipwrights, CP9 (hidden)
- **Key Events:**
  - Arrive at Water 7 to repair the Going Merry
  - Meet Iceburg — mayor and head of Galley-La Company, the world's best shipwrights
  - Devastating news: the Going Merry cannot be repaired. The keel is broken. The ship is dying.
  - Harry refuses to accept it. Usopp refuses even harder — the Merry was a gift from Kaya, it's everything to him
  - The crew's money (200 million berries from Skypiea gold) is stolen by the Franky Family — a gang of ship dismantlers led by Franky (a cyborg)
  - Usopp goes to get the money back alone and gets beaten badly
  - Harry decides to get a new ship. Usopp SNAPS. He challenges Harry to a duel for the Going Merry.
- **Scenes:**
  1. **The City of Water** — Water 7 is stunning — a Venice-like city built on water, with canals instead of streets, water elevators called Bull lifts, and beautiful architecture. The Galley-La Company runs everything — shipbuilding is the city's lifeblood. Let Harry explore the city and ride the canals, marvel at the water elevators, and eat local food.
  2. **Meeting Iceburg** — Iceburg is the mayor and head of Galley-La. He is calm, professional, and commands immense respect. The crew brings the Going Merry for repairs. Iceburg's shipwrights inspect the Merry and deliver the devastating news: the keel — the spine of the ship — is broken beyond repair. The Merry will not survive another voyage. She is dying.
  3. **The Crew Divides** — Harry is stunned but accepts the truth: they need a new ship. Usopp cannot accept it. The Merry was a gift from Kaya — it is his connection to Syrup Village, to his past, to the person who believed in him. Usopp: "We can't just throw her away!" Harry: "She can't sail anymore." The argument builds. The tension in the crew is palpable. Let Harry try to explain his decision.
  4. **The Franky Family** — While the crew argues, the 200 million berries (their Skypiea gold money) is stolen by the Franky Family — a gang of ship dismantlers and bounty hunters led by a mysterious cyborg named Franky. They are thugs, loud and brash. Usopp was carrying the money. He chases the Franky Family alone to get it back. They beat him savagely and leave him bloody in the street.
  5. **The Crew Retaliates** — Harry, Zoro, Sanji, and Chopper storm the Franky Family's hideout and demolish it. They crush every member. But the money is gone — Franky already spent it on supplies. The crew returns to find Usopp, beaten and ashamed. This is Usopp's breaking point.
  6. **Usopp's Challenge** — Harry announces he has decided to get a new ship. Usopp explodes. He accuses Harry of abandoning the Merry, of not caring, of being a bad captain. Harry tries to stay calm but Usopp pushes harder. Finally, Usopp says the words: "If this is how you treat your ship... then I quit. And I challenge you for the Going Merry. Captain vs crew member. A duel." The crew is frozen. Let Harry react to the challenge from his friend.

**Chapter 19: Water 7 (Part 2) — Harry vs Usopp**
- **Setting:** Water 7, the shore by the Going Merry
- **Key Characters:** Harry, Usopp
- **Key Events:**
  - Harry and Usopp fight. Really fight. Usopp uses every trick he has — impact dials, smoke stars, caltrops. He knows he can't win but he fights anyway
  - Harry wins. Usopp leaves the crew. Takes the Merry.
  - The crew is devastated. Harry is in tears but holds firm — a captain can't be pushed around
  - That night, Iceburg is shot. Robin is the suspect. Robin is seen with masked agents.
  - Robin tells Harry: "Don't follow me. Goodbye."
  - The truth: CP9 — a secret World Government assassination unit — has been hiding in Water 7 for five years, disguised as Galley-La shipwrights. They want Robin for her ability to read Poneglyphs. They've threatened to use a Buster Call (complete military annihilation) on the crew if Robin doesn't surrender
  - Robin is sacrificing herself to save the crew
- **Scenes:**
  1. **The Duel** — Night. The shore by the Going Merry. Harry and Usopp face each other. This is not a game. Usopp has prepared — impact dials, smoke stars, caltrops, rotten eggs, pepper bombs. He knows he cannot win in a straight fight. He has to be clever. And he is. Usopp fights with everything — every trick, every trap, every ounce of cunning. He hits Harry with impact dials that send shockwaves through his rubber body. He blinds him with smoke. He trips him with caltrops. Let Harry fight Usopp — and feel the pain of fighting a friend.
  2. **Usopp's Last Stand** — Usopp is outmatched in raw power. Harry is stronger, faster, tougher. But Usopp refuses to stay down. He gets up, bleeding, broken, and fires again. And again. He screams about the Merry, about being weak, about being left behind. "I know I'm not strong! I know I can't keep up! But I can't just let you throw her away!" The crew watches from the shadows. Nami is crying. Sanji clenches his fists. Chopper sobs. Zoro stands rigid.
  3. **Harry Ends It** — Harry hits Usopp with a Gum Gum Bullet — one clean hit that ends the fight. Usopp crumples. Harry stands over him, tears streaming down his face. He wants to say sorry. He wants to take it back. But he is the captain. A captain cannot be swayed on a decision that affects the crew's survival. Harry walks away. "The Going Merry is yours. Take care of her." Usopp lies on the shore. He is no longer a Straw Hat.
  4. **The Crew's Darkest Night** — The crew returns to their lodging in silence. Nobody eats. Nobody speaks. Harry sits alone, hat over his eyes. The crew is broken. The family has fractured. This is worse than any villain, any battle. Let Harry sit with this pain.
  5. **Iceburg Is Shot** — That same night, Iceburg is shot in his office. The suspects: Nico Robin and a group of masked figures. The city turns on the crew. Robin is seen with the attackers — CP9, though nobody knows their identity yet.
  6. **Robin's Goodbye** — Harry finds Robin on the bridge. She looks at him with cold, empty eyes: "Do not follow me. Forget about me. Goodbye." She walks away into the rain. Harry shouts after her. She does not turn around. Something is very wrong — Robin would not do this willingly. But why? Let Harry decide what to believe — Robin's words or his instincts.
  7. **CP9 — The Hidden Assassins** — The truth emerges: CP9 is a secret World Government assassination unit. Four of their agents have been living undercover in Water 7 for FIVE YEARS — disguised as Galley-La shipwrights. They want Robin because she can read Poneglyphs. They have threatened to call a Buster Call (total military annihilation) on the Straw Hats if Robin does not surrender. Robin is sacrificing herself to save her crew.
- **Emotional Beat:** Harry vs Usopp — the crew's darkest moment. The captain and his friend tearing each other apart. Robin's silent sacrifice. The crew breaking apart.
- **Anime Moments:** Usopp firing impact dials at Harry while crying, Harry walking away after winning, Robin saying goodbye in the rain

**Chapter 20: Water 7 (Part 3) — CP9 Revealed**
- **Setting:** Water 7, Galley-La headquarters
- **Key Characters:** Harry, crew, CP9 (Rob Lucci, Kaku, Kalifa, Blueno), Franky
- **Key Events:**
  - CP9 reveals themselves — Rob Lucci, Kaku, Kalifa, and Blueno have been undercover for years
  - Rob Lucci is terrifyingly powerful — Leopard-Leopard Fruit, master of Rokushiki (six superhuman martial arts)
  - CP9 beats Harry and the crew badly, takes Robin and Franky, and heads to Enies Lobby — the judicial island of the World Government
  - Franky's backstory: He was Tom's apprentice. Tom was the shipwright who built Roger's ship. Tom was executed by the World Government. Franky tried to stop the train and was destroyed — rebuilt himself as a cyborg
  - The crew recovers. They're going after Robin. All of them.
  - The sea train — Puffing Tom — is their ride to Enies Lobby
  - Sanji goes ahead on the train alone, fighting through cars of agents
- **Scenes:**
  1. **The Masks Come Off** — At Galley-La headquarters, the truth is revealed. Rob Lucci — the quiet, pigeon-holding carpenter — is CP9's strongest agent. Kaku — the friendly long-nosed shipwright — is CP9. Kalifa — Iceburg's secretary — is CP9. Blueno — the bartender — is CP9. Five years of perfect cover, shattered in an instant. The people Harry's crew trusted were enemies the entire time.
  2. **Rob Lucci** — Lucci is terrifying. Leopard-Leopard Fruit (Zoan type) — he transforms into a leopard-human hybrid. He is a master of Rokushiki — six superhuman martial arts (Shave/speed, Iron Body/defense, Finger Pistol/piercing, Tempest Kick/ranged slash, Moon Walk/air walk, Paper Art/dodging). He is cold, emotionless, and lives to kill. He defeats Harry with contemptuous ease. Finger Pistol through Harry's chest. Harry goes down.
  3. **CP9 Takes Robin and Franky** — CP9 captures Robin (who surrendered willingly) and Franky (who they want for knowledge of Pluton's blueprints). They board the sea train — Puffing Tom — headed for Enies Lobby, the World Government's judicial island. The crew is beaten, scattered, and broken.
  4. **Franky's Backstory** — Franky is revealed to be Cutty Flam — the apprentice of the legendary shipwright Tom. Tom built Gol D. Roger's ship, the Oro Jackson. Tom was put on trial by the World Government. As payment for his "crime" of building Roger's ship, Tom offered to build the sea train. When the Government came to execute him anyway, young Franky tried to stop the train with his body — and was destroyed. He rebuilt himself as a cyborg. He has Tom's blueprints for Pluton (passed down as insurance against the World Government). Let Harry learn Franky's story and feel the connection to Roger.
  5. **The Crew Recovers** — Bruised, bleeding, humiliated. But Harry stands up. "We're going to get Robin back." There is no debate. No hesitation. They are going to Enies Lobby. The sea train is their ride. The Galley-La workers — the real ones, not the spies — rally behind the crew.
  6. **Sanji on the Train** — Sanji boarded the sea train ahead of everyone, alone. He fights through cars full of Government agents, Marine escorts, and CP9 operatives. One man against an army, on a moving train in the rain. He is magnificent. Let Harry learn what Sanji did while the others were recovering.
  7. **The Ride to War** — The crew boards the next sea train — Rocketman, a prototype that goes too fast and cannot stop. They ride it through the storm toward Enies Lobby. On the train with them: Galley-La shipwrights, the Franky Family (who want their boss back), and determination. The storm rages. The train screams across the ocean. They are heading to war with the World Government.
- **Emotional Beat:** The betrayal of trusted allies. Rob Lucci's terrifying power. The crew's determination to save Robin despite everything.
- **Anime Moments:** Rob Lucci transforming into his leopard form, Sanji fighting alone through the sea train, the Rocketman charging through the storm

**Chapter 21: Enies Lobby (Part 1) — Declaration of War**
- **Setting:** Enies Lobby — the World Government's judicial island, the island that never sees darkness
- **Key Characters:** Harry, crew (minus Usopp, plus Franky and Galley-La allies), Robin, Spandam, CP9
- **Key Events:**
  - The crew arrives at Enies Lobby — a fortress with 10,000 soldiers, the Gates of Justice, and CP9
  - Robin's full backstory: Ohara — an island of scholars who studied the Void Century (forbidden history). The World Government ordered a Buster Call and destroyed the entire island. Robin was 8 years old. She was the sole survivor. She's been hunted her entire life. Every person who ever helped her was killed. She believes she brings death to everyone she cares about.
  - Robin stands on the far side of a gap, surrounded by CP9. She says: "I can't come with you. I don't want to be saved. Because I... I know that eventually you'll find me to be a burden and betray me."
  - Harry's response: He orders Usopp (who is secretly there, wearing a mask as "Sogeking") to shoot down the World Government flag.
  - The flag burns. Harry shouts across the gap:
  - **"ROBIN! WE'RE YOUR FRIENDS! WE'D BURN DOWN THE WHOLE WORLD FOR YOU! TELL US YOU WANT TO LIVE!"**
  - Robin, in tears, screams: **"I WANT TO LIVE! TAKE ME TO THE SEA WITH YOU!"**
  - The crew charges into Enies Lobby
- **Scenes:**
  1. **The Fortress** — Enies Lobby is terrifying — a judicial island that never sees darkness (perpetual daylight from a hole in the sky), surrounded by a massive whirlpool, defended by 10,000 soldiers, the Gates of Justice, and CP9. The crew crashes through the front gate on the Rocketman. Ten thousand Marines mobilize. Let Harry see the scale of what they are attacking — and charge in anyway.
  2. **The Assault** — The crew (plus Galley-La, Franky Family, and the giants Oimo and Kashii who switch sides when they learn the truth) storms the island. Harry punches through platoons. Zoro cuts through squads. Sanji kicks through barricades. Usopp — who is NOT officially part of the crew anymore — appears wearing a mask and cape, calling himself "Sogeking, the King of Snipers from Sniper Island." Everyone knows it is Usopp. Nobody says anything.
  3. **Robin's Backstory — Ohara (Part 1)** — The story of Robin's past unfolds. Ohara was an island of scholars — the greatest library in the world. The scholars studied the Poneglyphs and the Void Century (800 years of erased history). The World Government declared this knowledge forbidden. Robin was eight years old, an outcast child with the Flower-Flower Fruit, mocked by other kids for being a "devil child."
  4. **Robin's Backstory — Ohara (Part 2)** — Young Robin's only friends were the scholars, especially Professor Clover and a giant named Jaguar D. Saul (a defecting Marine who washed up on the island). Saul taught Robin to laugh: "Dereshishishi!" The World Government ordered a Buster Call — complete annihilation. Ten warships. The library burned. The scholars died. Saul was frozen by Aokiji. Robin ran to the evacuation boat. Aokiji let her go — one survivor, as Saul's dying wish.
  5. **Robin's Backstory — 20 Years Alone (Part 3)** — Robin spent 20 years running. Every person who helped her was hunted down and killed by the Government. Every friend, every protector, every kind soul — dead because of her. She learned to trust no one. She learned to use people and leave before they died for her. She joined Baroque Works because she had nowhere else to go. And now she believes the Straw Hats will die because of her, just like everyone else. She surrendered to CP9 to save them.
  6. **The Bridge** — Robin stands on the far side of a judicial gap, handcuffed, surrounded by CP9 and Spandam (the cowardly CP9 commander). She tells the crew: "I cannot come with you. Do not save me. Eventually you will betray me too." She has given up. She has accepted death rather than risk more people dying for her.
  7. **Burn the Flag** — Harry's response. He looks at Robin across the gap. He does not argue. He does not beg. He turns to Sogeking (Usopp) and gives one order: "Shoot down that flag." Usopp loads a flaming ammunition into his slingshot, aims at the World Government flag flying above Enies Lobby — the symbol of the government that rules the entire world — and shoots. The flag catches fire. It burns. The crew watches it fall. This is a declaration of war against the World Government. The entire world will know what the Straw Hats did here.
  8. **"I WANT TO LIVE!"** — Harry shouts across the gap: "ROBIN! Say you want to live! Say it!" Robin breaks. Twenty years of walls crumble. The tears come. She screams with everything she has: "I WANT TO LIVE! TAKE ME TO THE SEA WITH YOU!" The crew charges. This is the single most iconic moment in One Piece.
- **Emotional Beat:** "I WANT TO LIVE!" — Robin's 20-year wall of isolation shattering in one scream. The crew declaring war on the entire World Government for one friend. Burning the flag. The single most iconic moment in One Piece.
- **Anime Moments:** The World Government flag burning, Robin screaming "I want to live!" with tears streaming, the crew charging across the gap

**Chapter 22: Enies Lobby (Part 2) — The Battles**
- **Setting:** Enies Lobby, the Tower of Justice
- **Key Characters:** All crew vs CP9 members
- **Key Events:**
  - Each crew member gets a 1v1 fight against a CP9 agent:
    - Nami vs Kalifa (Bubble-Bubble Fruit)
    - Usopp/Sogeking vs Jabra (Wolf-Wolf Fruit) — fighting alongside Sanji
    - Sanji vs Jabra — Sanji unlocks Diable Jambe (flaming kicks)
    - Chopper vs Kumadori — Chopper loses control in Monster Point
    - Franky vs Fukurou
    - Zoro vs Kaku (Giraffe-Giraffe Fruit) — Zoro uses Asura (nine-sword style illusion) for the first time
  - Each fight pushes the crew to their absolute limits
  - Spandam (the cowardly CP9 leader) drags Robin toward the Gate of Justice
- **Scenes:**
  1. **The Tower of Justice** — The crew reaches the Tower of Justice. CP9 waits — each agent in a separate room. The crew must fight through them to reach Robin. Franky is freed and joins the fight. Each crew member faces their match.
  2. **Nami vs Kalifa** — Kalifa has the Bubble-Bubble Fruit — she creates soap bubbles that make anyone slippery and powerless. Nami is stripped of her ability to fight or even stand. She is humiliated. But Nami uses her Clima-Tact to summon thunder and blasts Kalifa with a Thunderbolt Tempo. Nami wins through intelligence and weather science.
  3. **Chopper vs Kumadori** — Kumadori is an eccentric fighter who uses Life Return (controlling his hair and body). Chopper uses his Rumble Ball transformations but cannot keep up. In desperation, Chopper takes a third Rumble Ball — triggering Monster Point, an uncontrollable giant form of immense power. He wins but loses all control and must be stopped by the crew afterward. The danger of Monster Point is established.
  4. **Franky vs Fukurou** — A brawl between two powerhouses. Franky uses his cyborg weapons — Coup de Vent (air cannon), Strong Right (rocket fist), and cola-powered attacks. He runs out of cola mid-fight and must refuel. A fun, loud fight that matches Franky's personality.
  5. **Sanji vs Jabra** — Jabra has the Wolf-Wolf Fruit — a vicious, fast predator. Sanji fights him with kicks alone (he never uses his hands — his hands are for cooking). Mid-fight, Sanji unlocks Diable Jambe — by spinning at extreme speed, his leg catches fire. His kicks become devastatingly powerful. He defeats Jabra with a flaming kick combo. A major power-up for Sanji.
  6. **Sogeking (Usopp) in Battle** — Usopp, still masked as Sogeking, fights alongside other crew members. He provides ranged support, snipes targets from impossible distances, and sets up tactical advantages. He is terrified the entire time but never runs.
  7. **Zoro vs Kaku** — Kaku ate the Giraffe-Giraffe Fruit — yes, a giraffe. It sounds ridiculous and IS ridiculous, but Kaku uses it with deadly effectiveness, extending his neck for long-range strikes. Zoro is pushed to his limits. He unleashes Asura — a terrifying illusion technique where Zoro appears to have six arms, three heads, and nine swords. One devastating strike — Asura: Ichibugin. Kaku falls. Zoro's most powerful technique yet.
  8. **Spandam Drags Robin** — While the fights rage, Spandam — the sniveling, cowardly, incompetent CP9 commander — drags Robin toward the Gate of Justice. He taunts her, hits her with the Elephant Sword (a sword that ate an Elephant fruit — yes, really), and demonstrates everything wrong with the World Government: cruel, petty power over the helpless. Robin endures in silence, waiting for her crew.
- **Emotional Beat:** Each crew member fighting beyond their limits for Robin. Sanji's Diable Jambe. Zoro's Asura. The crew earning their way to their friend.
- **Anime Moments:** Sanji's leg catching fire for Diable Jambe, Zoro's Asura nine-sword illusion, Chopper's terrifying Monster Point

**Chapter 23: Enies Lobby (Part 3) — Harry vs Rob Lucci**
- **Setting:** Enies Lobby, the Tower of Justice
- **Key Characters:** Harry, Rob Lucci
- **Key Events:**
  - Harry vs Rob Lucci — the greatest fight of the first half of One Piece
  - Rob Lucci is a killing machine. Leopard form, Rokushiki mastered, utterly ruthless
  - Harry unveils Gear 2 (pumps blood faster, insane speed and power, steam comes off his body) and Gear 3 (inflates his bones to giant size for devastating blows)
  - Even with both new Gears, Lucci keeps getting up. Harry is beaten to a pulp. Can barely stand.
  - Usopp — from across the island — screams at Harry through a Den Den Mushi: "GET UP, HARRY! YOU'RE THE MAN WHO'S GOING TO BE KING OF THE PIRATES!"
  - Harry stands. One final attack: Gum Gum Jet Gatling — an onslaught of Gear 2 punches that finally puts Lucci down
  - The crew escapes as the Buster Call arrives — ten warships bombarding the island
  - The Going Merry appears from nowhere to save them — sailing itself with no one aboard
  - They escape on the Merry one last time
- **Scenes:**
  1. **Harry Faces Lucci** — Lucci stands between Harry and Robin. Leopard hybrid form. Rokushiki mastered. Finger Pistol pierces Harry's rubber body. Iron Body makes Lucci nearly invulnerable. Harry is getting destroyed.
  2. **Gear 2** — Harry pumps his blood faster through his rubber vessels. Steam rises from his skin. "Gear Second." Jet Pistol — ten times normal speed. Harry lands hits for the first time. Jet Bazooka, Jet Gatling. Massive power but burns through stamina fast.
  3. **Gear 3** — Harry inflates his bones with air — his fist swells to giant size. "Gear Third." Gigant Pistol — a fist the size of a building. But afterward Harry shrinks to chibi-size temporarily.
  4. **Lucci's Assault** — Rokuougan — a shockwave that hits from inside, bypassing rubber. Harry vomits blood. His organs are damaged. He falls. He cannot move. Lucci walks toward Robin.
  5. **Usopp's Voice** — From across the island, through a Den Den Mushi: "Harry! GET UP! You are the man who will be KING OF THE PIRATES! There is no way you can lose here!" Harry hears his friend. His fingers twitch. He stands.
  6. **Jet Gatling** — Gear 2. Gum Gum Jet Gatling — hundreds of high-speed punches. Lucci cannot dodge them all. One final punch. Lucci falls. He does not get up.
  7. **The Buster Call** — Ten warships bombard Enies Lobby. Fire everywhere. No way out.
  8. **The Going Merry** — From the flames — a ship. No one at the helm. The Going Merry sailed herself to save her crew one last time. The Klabautermann — the spirit of the ship — brought her. The crew leaps aboard. They escape through the bombardment. One last voyage.
- **Emotional Beat:** Harry getting up because of Usopp's voice. Jet Gatling. The Going Merry sailing herself to save the crew.
- **Anime Moments:** Steam rising as Gear 2 activates, the Jet Gatling barrage, the Going Merry appearing through the flames

**Chapter 24: Farewell, Going Merry**
- **Setting:** The sea outside Enies Lobby
- **Key Characters:** Harry, crew, the Going Merry
- **Key Events:**
  - The Merry saved them but she's falling apart. She can't sail anymore.
  - The crew gives her a Viking funeral at sea. Harry sets her ablaze.
  - The Merry speaks (the spirit of the ship): "I'm sorry. I wanted to carry you just a little further."
  - Everyone cries. Harry: "I'M SORRY! I'M SORRY WE BROKE YOU! YOU WERE THE BEST SHIP EVER!"
  - The Merry sinks into the sea, burning.
  - Back at Water 7 — the crew recovers. Bounties updated for everyone.
  - Franky builds the crew a new ship: the Thousand Sunny — a masterpiece with a lion figurehead
  - Usopp wants to rejoin but is too proud to just come back. Harry insists he must apologize (a captain's authority matters). Usopp finally breaks down: "I'M SORRY! PLEASE LET ME SAIL WITH YOU AGAIN!"
  - Franky officially joins the crew as the shipwright
  - Harry's new bounty: 300 million berries
- **Scenes:**
  1. **The Merry Cannot Go On** — The crew escapes the Buster Call on the Going Merry. But the ship is breaking apart in real time. The keel snaps. The mast cracks. Wood splinters under their feet. She carried them one final time, and now she is dying. The crew stands on the deck of their first real ship and knows this is the end.
  2. **The Viking Funeral** — They transfer to a Marine ship they commandeered. Harry stands before the Going Merry one last time. He lights the fire himself. The Merry burns on the open sea. The flames climb the mast, catch the sail, consume the figurehead.
  3. **The Merry Speaks** — As the Merry burns, a voice emerges — the spirit of the ship, the Klabautermann. A soft, sad, grateful voice: "I am sorry. I wanted to carry you all just a little further." The entire crew breaks down. Chopper sobs. Nami covers her face. Zoro turns away. Sanji hides his tears. Usopp — who fought Harry for this ship — screams. Harry, tears pouring, screams back: "I'M SORRY! WE BROKE YOU! YOU WERE THE BEST SHIP EVER!" The Merry sinks into the sea, burning. Let Harry feel this loss — this is the death of a friend, not a thing.
  4. **Recovery in Water 7** — The crew recovers at Water 7. Wounds heal. Spirits slowly lift. Iceburg is alive and recovering from his shooting. The city, once hostile, now respects the crew for exposing CP9.
  5. **Franky Builds the Thousand Sunny** — Franky uses the 200 million berries (the money the Franky Family stole) to buy Adam Wood — the rarest, strongest shipbuilding material in the world. He builds the crew a new ship: the Thousand Sunny. She is magnificent — a lion-headed figurehead, Coup de Burst propulsion (cola-powered cannon jump), a lawn deck, an aquarium, a kitchen Sanji adores, a sick bay for Chopper, a library for Robin, a workshop for Franky and Usopp. She is their new home.
  6. **Usopp's Apology** — Usopp wants to rejoin the crew. He is hanging around, trying to casually run into them. But Harry is firm: Usopp left. He challenged the captain and lost. If he wants back, he has to apologize. Zoro supports this (a captain cannot be weak). The crew waits. Usopp is too proud. He tries to play it off. He pretends nothing happened. But as the Sunny prepares to sail, Usopp stands on the shore, tears streaming, and screams: "I AM SORRY! I WAS WRONG! PLEASE LET ME SAIL WITH YOU AGAIN!" Harry, already crying, stretches his arm and pulls Usopp aboard: "WHAT TOOK YOU SO LONG, IDIOT!" The crew is whole again.
  7. **Franky Joins** — Franky wants to go but claims he cannot leave Water 7. The Franky Family and Galley-La workers steal his swimming trunks (his only clothing) and hold them hostage on the Thousand Sunny. Franky, naked and chasing them, ends up on the ship as it sails away. He gives in: "FINE! I will build you the greatest ship in the world!" Franky officially joins as the shipwright.
  8. **New Bounties** — The crew gets updated bounties. Harry: 300 million berries. Zoro: 120 million. Nami: 16 million. Usopp: 30 million (as "Sogeking"). Sanji: 77 million (his photo is STILL a terrible sketch). Chopper: 50 berries. Robin: 80 million. Franky: 44 million. The world now knows the Straw Hats declared war on the World Government.
- **Emotional Beat:** The Going Merry's death. "I wanted to carry you just a little further." Usopp's apology. The crew whole again. The Thousand Sunny as a new beginning.
- **Anime Moments:** The Going Merry burning at sea, the Merry's spirit speaking, Usopp screaming his apology from the shore
- **Crew After Chapter:** Harry, Zoro, Nami, Usopp, Sanji, Chopper, Robin, Franky
- **Ship:** Thousand Sunny

**Chapter 25: Thriller Bark — The Undead Island**
- **Setting:** Thriller Bark — a massive ship/island in the Florian Triangle, covered in fog and monsters
- **Key Characters:** Harry, crew, Brook, Gecko Moria (Shadow-Shadow Fruit), Oars, Bartholomew Kuma
- **Key Events:**
  - The crew enters the Florian Triangle — a sea of fog and ghost ships
  - They meet Brook — a living skeleton, musician, Devil Fruit user (Revive-Revive Fruit). He died and came back, but by the time his soul found his body, it was just bones. He's been alone for 50 years.
  - Brook's backstory: His old crew, the Rumbar Pirates, made a promise to Laboon (the whale at Reverse Mountain!) that they'd return. They all died. Brook survived with the Devil Fruit. He carries their last song on a Tone Dial — recorded as they died, one by one: "Binks' Sake"
  - Thriller Bark: Gecko Moria steals shadows with his Devil Fruit and puts them into zombies. He steals Harry's shadow. Without it, sunlight will vaporize Harry.
  - The crew fights an army of zombies and Moria's commanders
  - Oars — a giant zombie powered by Harry's shadow. The entire crew must fight together to take him down
  - Harry defeats Moria with a new technique
  - **Kuma appears.** A Warlord. Paw-Paw Fruit. He's been ordered to eliminate the Straw Hats.
  - Zoro's defining moment: He offers his own life for Harry's. Kuma pushes all of Harry's pain into Zoro. Zoro absorbs it all and stands in a pool of his own blood. Sanji finds him. "What happened?" Zoro: "Nothing happened."
  - Brook joins the crew — so he can return to Laboon and fulfill the Rumbar Pirates' promise
- **Scenes:**
  1. **The Florian Triangle** — The Sunny sails into dense fog. Ghost ships drift past. Usopp, Nami, and Chopper cling to each other in terror. A skeleton walks onto their deck: "May I see your panties?" This is Brook.
  2. **Brook** — He ate the Revive-Revive Fruit. When he died his soul returned but his body was bones. Alone for 50 years. Cheerful, polite, skull jokes. He cannot join — his shadow was stolen.
  3. **Thriller Bark** — The largest ship in the world. Halloween-themed. Gecko Moria, Shadow-Shadow Fruit. He steals shadows and creates zombies. Without your shadow, sunlight dissolves you.
  4. **Shadows Stolen** — Moria steals Harry's shadow, puts it into Oars — a giant hundreds of feet tall with Harry's personality. Harry must avoid sunlight.
  5. **Brook's Backstory** — His crew, the Rumbar Pirates, promised baby Laboon they would return. They all died. Their last song — Binks' Sake — was recorded on a Tone Dial, voices fading as each one dies mid-song. Brook has been alone 50 years carrying it.
  6. **The Crew vs Oars** — The entire crew fights Oars together. Zoro cuts, Sanji kicks, Franky shoots, Nami controls weather, Robin uses her arms. First true combined battle.
  7. **Harry vs Moria** — Harry absorbs 100 shadows (Nightmare Harry). Demolishes Moria. Moria falls.
  8. **Kuma Appears** — Bartholomew Kuma. Warlord. Paw-Paw Fruit. The exhausted crew cannot fight him.
  9. **Zoro's Sacrifice** — Zoro offers his life for Harry's. Kuma extracts all of Harry's pain into a bubble. Zoro steps in. Every wound floods his body. Sanji finds him in a pool of blood. "What happened?" Zoro: "Nothing happened."
  10. **Brook Joins** — Shadow recovered. He plays Binks' Sake on his violin. The crew sings along. He will return to Laboon. Nine members.
- **Emotional Beat:** "Nothing happened." Zoro's sacrifice. Brook's 50-year solitude. Binks' Sake.
- **Anime Moments:** The Rumbar Pirates singing as they die, Zoro standing in blood, Brook playing violin on the Sunny
- **Crew After Chapter:** Harry, Zoro, Nami, Usopp, Sanji, Chopper, Robin, Franky, Brook

---

### SAGA 4: SUMMIT WAR (Chapters 26-33)

The world breaks. The crew is shattered. Harry faces the greatest war in history. Loss. Real loss.

---

**Chapter 26: Sabaody Archipelago (Part 1) — The Lawless Grove**
- **Setting:** Sabaody Archipelago — an island of mangrove trees near the Red Line, where pirates prepare to enter the New World
- **Key Characters:** Harry, crew, Silvers Rayleigh (Roger's first mate), the Eleven Supernovas (Worst Generation), Celestial Dragons, Admiral Kizaru
- **Key Events:**
  1. **Arrival at the Archipelago** — The Thousand Sunny surfaces near the massive mangrove trees of Sabaody. Bubbles float everywhere — the island's resin creates natural bubbles that drift through the air. Chopper tries to catch them, Usopp inflates one and rides it before popping and falling. Harry declares it the coolest island ever. Nami explains this is the last stop before the New World — they need to coat the ship in resin to travel underwater to Fishman Island.
  2. **Duval and the Flying Fish Riders** — The crew encounters Duval, a man whose face matches Sanji's terrible wanted poster sketch. After a comical confrontation, Sanji kicks his face into a new shape — Duval becomes handsome. He pledges his Flying Fish Riders to serve the Straw Hats out of gratitude.
  3. **Meeting Camie, Hachi, and Pappag** — The crew reunites with Hachi — the octopus fishman from Arlong Park, now reformed and running a takoyaki stand. Harry bears no grudge and gobbles down his takoyaki. Hachi introduces Camie (a bubbly young mermaid) and Pappag (a talking starfish fashion designer). Hachi warns them: "Whatever you do, do not anger the Celestial Dragons."
  4. **Exploring the Lawless Zone** — The crew splits up. Harry, Chopper, and Brook ride bubble bikes, eat cotton candy, bounce on resin trampolines. Nami and Robin notice slave collars on sale in a shop. Zoro immediately gets lost (Grove 1 instead of Grove 13). Sanji flirts with every woman in sight. Franky examines coating technology. Fun on the surface, but darkness lurks beneath.
  5. **The Eleven Supernovas** — Harry bumps into other rookie pirates. Eustass Kid pins Marines to walls with magnetic powers. Trafalgar Law watches Harry with quiet interest. Jewelry Bonney devours a restaurant's worth of food. Basil Hawkins reads tarot cards. Scratchmen Apoo plays music that slices buildings. X Drake, Urouge, Capone Bege, Killer — each radiates danger. Harry grins: "The Grand Line has so many strong people!"
  6. **Shakky's Rip-Off Bar** — Hachi leads part of the crew to Shakky's bar. Shakky mentions her partner — a coating mechanic named Rayleigh. Robin's eyes widen: "Silvers Rayleigh. The Dark King. First mate of Gold Roger." The room goes quiet.
  7. **The Slave Auction House** — Camie is kidnapped by slave traders and taken to the Human Auction House. The crew races to save her. Celestial Dragons sit in VIP seats wearing bubble helmets, bidding on slaves. It is horrifying. Hachi begs them not to cause a scene: attacking a Celestial Dragon summons a Marine Admiral automatically.
  8. **Hachi Is Shot** — Camie is brought onstage as the star item. Hachi rushes the stage to save her, revealing himself as a fishman. Saint Charlos shoots Hachi in the chest. Hachi collapses: "I am sorry... I told you not to cause trouble..." Everyone stares at Harry.
  9. **Harry Punches a God** — Harry walks forward. The crew tries to warn him. Harry does not slow down. He punches Saint Charlos in the face. The Celestial Dragon crashes through a wall. Dead silence. Then chaos. Kid and Law both grin from the crowd. Harry: "Let's get Camie out of here."
  10. **Rayleigh Appears** — An old man emerges from backstage — he let himself be captured to rob the auction house. He releases Conqueror's Haki, knocking out every guard. This is Silvers Rayleigh, first mate of the Pirate King. He smiles: "Not bad, young man. You remind me of my old captain." He frees Camie's explosive collar. Harry stares — this is someone who has seen the One Piece.
- **Emotional Beat:** Harry punching the Celestial Dragon — standing against the most powerful bloodline in the world because they hurt his friend. No hesitation. Just righteous fury.
- **Anime Moments:** 1) The Eleven Supernovas assembled; 2) Harry's fist connecting with Saint Charlos's face; 3) Rayleigh unleashing Conqueror's Haki.
- **Crew After Chapter:** Harry, Zoro, Nami, Usopp, Sanji, Chopper, Robin, Franky, Brook — Marine Admiral incoming

**Chapter 27: Sabaody Archipelago (Part 2) — The Crew Vanishes**
- **Setting:** Sabaody Archipelago — the groves becoming a war zone
- **Key Characters:** Harry, crew, Kizaru (Admiral, Light-Light Fruit), Sentomaru, Pacifistas, Bartholomew Kuma, Rayleigh
- **Scenes:**
  1. **Rayleigh's Offer** — In Shakky's bar, Rayleigh tells the crew about Roger. He offers to answer any question about the One Piece, but Harry stops him: "I do not want to know. If you told me, I would quit being a pirate. We will find it ourselves." Rayleigh laughs, deeply impressed. He agrees to coat their ship, but it will take three days. Three days they may not have — the Marines are already coming.
  2. **Admiral Kizaru Arrives** — The sky flashes. A beam of light shoots down and explodes a mangrove tree. Admiral Borsalino — "Kizaru" — has arrived. The Light-Light Fruit. He speaks in a slow, lazy drawl but moves at the speed of light. He kicks a Supernova across the island in a blur. He is completely untouchable. The crew watches from hiding, terrified. This is a completely different level of power.
  3. **Sentomaru and the Pacifistas** — Sentomaru arrives with Pacifistas — cyborg replicas of Kuma. They are enormous and fire laser beams. The crew fights one Pacifista together — Zoro, Sanji, and Harry all hitting it at once — and barely bring it down. Then a second appears. And a third. They are surrounded and outmatched.
  4. **Scattered and Desperate** — The crew splits up and runs. Kizaru appears in front of Zoro and casually kicks him through trees. Zoro is bleeding badly. Rayleigh appears and blocks Kizaru's next attack with a Haki-coated sword: "Go! Take your crew and run!" But there is nowhere to run.
  5. **The Real Kuma Appears** — Bartholomew Kuma — the real one, not a copy — appears among the crew. His paw pads can repel anything, even people. He touches Zoro. Zoro vanishes — launched to an unknown island on the other side of the world. The crew screams.
  6. **One by One** — Kuma moves methodically. Brook — gone. Usopp — gone. Sanji tries to kick him mid-attack — gone. Franky charges with weapons — gone. Nami runs crying, reaching for Harry — gone. Chopper transforms into Monster Point — a single touch — gone. Robin restrains him with a thousand arms — he breaks free — gone. Harry watches each one disappear, screaming their names, running toward each vanishing silhouette. He cannot reach a single one.
  7. **Harry Is Last** — Harry stands alone, panting, crying, surrounded by empty ground. Kuma walks toward him. Harry collapses to his knees: "I could not save a single one of them..." Kuma, quietly: "We will never meet again. Farewell." He touches Harry. The world stretches. Harry is launched into the sky.
  8. **Alone in the Sky** — Harry flies for three days and three nights, over oceans and islands. He is helpless, alone, and for the first time, without hope. He replays the moment — every crew member vanishing, one by one. The boy who would be King of the Pirates could not save a single friend.
- **Emotional Beat:** The crew vanishing one by one. Harry reaching for each person and failing. The silence after the last one disappears. This is rock bottom.
- **Anime Moments:** 1) Kuma touching each crew member as they vanish in flashes of light; 2) Harry on his knees, alone in the empty grove; 3) The wide shot of Harry flying through the sky, a tiny figure against the vast world.
- **Crew After Chapter:** SCATTERED. Every member on a different island. Harry is alone.

**Chapter 28: Amazon Lily — The Island of Women**
- **Setting:** Amazon Lily — an island of warrior women in the Calm Belt
- **Key Characters:** Harry, Boa Hancock (Snake Princess, Warlord), Boa Sandersonia, Boa Marigold, Marguerite, Elder Nyon, the Kuja Pirates
- **Scenes:**
  1. **Crash Landing** — Harry smashes through the jungle canopy and lands in a river on Amazon Lily. He is battered, exhausted, and alone. The jungle is lush and beautiful. Strange animals watch him. He wanders, looking for food and people, calling out for anyone. The silence of being without his crew is deafening.
  2. **Captured by the Kuja** — Marguerite and a group of Kuja warriors find Harry. They have never seen a man before — Amazon Lily is forbidden to men. They poke his face, pull his rubber skin in wonder, and debate whether he is a monster or animal. Harry tries to be friendly. They confiscate his clothes to examine them. Comedy ensues as Harry runs around trying to get dressed while the warriors treat him like a zoo exhibit.
